$$\begin{equation}p(t)=\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}(t)}\end{equation}$$

éå¹³è¡¡å®šæ€ï¼šç»éªŒè¡¨æ˜ï¼Œä½“ç³»å¤„äºç¯å¢ƒä¸å˜çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œç»è¿‡ä¸€æ®µæ—¶é—´åï¼Œä½“ç³»å¿…å°†è¾¾åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªå®è§‚ä¸Šä¸éšæ—¶é—´å˜åŒ–çš„çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œå°½ç®¡ä¸ä¸€å®šæ˜¯å¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼Œä½†ä½“ç³»å°†é•¿ä¹…çš„ä¿æŒè¿™ç§çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œè¿™ç§çŠ¶æ€ç§°ä¸ºéå¹³è¡¡å®šæ€ï¼ˆå®šæ€ã€ç¨³æ€ã€å®šå¸¸æ€stationary stateï¼‰ï¼Œæè¿°ä¸ºï¼š$\frac{\partial \langle B\rangle}{\partial t}= 0$ï¼ˆæ³¨æ„ï¼Œåªæ˜¯æ—¶é—´çš„åå¯¼ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯å…¨å¯¼ï¼‰ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ï¼šåœ¨ä¸¤ä¸ªå…·æœ‰ç¨³å®šæ¸©å·®ä¸­å½¢æˆçš„çƒ­æµï¼Œæ˜¯å®šæ€ã€‚

å¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼šå¤„äºå®šæ€ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å…¶ç¯å¢ƒçš„å®è§‚çŠ¶æ€å®è§‚çŠ¶æ€ä¹Ÿä¸å˜ï¼Œåˆ™è¿™ä¸ªä½“ç³»ç§°ä¸ºå¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€ã€‚ä½“ç³»çš„æ‰€æœ‰å®è§‚æ€§è´¨éšæ—¶é—´ä¸å˜åŒ–ï¼š$\frac{\partial \langle B\rangle}{\partial t}=0$ã€‚å¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€çš„ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå†…éƒ¨å…è®¸å‡ºç°æŸç§å¾®è§‚ä¸å‡åŒ€ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯ä¸å…è®¸å‡ºç°æµï¼ˆçƒ­æµã€ç²’å­æµç­‰ï¼‰ã€‚

éå¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼šä½“ç³»æ‰€å¤„çš„å®è§‚çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œéä¸Šè¿°çš„å¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼Œå‡å¤„äºéå¹³è¡¡æ€ã€‚

å¼›è±«è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼šå¤„äºéå¹³è¡¡æ€çš„ä½“ç³»æœ‰è‡ªå‘è¶‹å‘å¹³è¡¡æ€çš„è¶‹åŠ¿ï¼Œè¿™ç§ä»éå¹³è¡¡æ€åˆ°å¹³è¡¡æ€çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ç§°ä¸ºå¼›è±«è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚

å¹¿å»¶é‡ä¸å¼ºåº¦é‡ï¼šæè¿°ä½“ç³»æ‰€éœ€çš„æ‰€æœ‰å®è§‚å‚é‡ã€‚ä¸ä½“ç³»è´¨é‡æœ‰å…³çš„ç§°ä¸ºå¹¿å»¶é‡ï¼Œä¸ä½“ç³»è´¨é‡æ— å…³çš„ç§°ä¸ºå¼ºåº¦é‡ã€‚

å¤–å‚é‡ä¸å†…å‚é‡ï¼šå®è§‚å‚é‡çš„å¦ä¸€ç§åˆ†ç±»æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œåªå–å†³äºç¯å¢ƒè€Œä¸ä½“ç³»æ— å…³çš„å®è§‚é‡ç§°ä¸ºå¤–å‚é‡ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ï¼šä½“ç³»ä½“ç§¯ã€ä½“ç³»å¤–å½¢ã€å¤–ç”µåœºã€å¤–ç£åœºï¼›å–å†³äºä½“ç³»å†…éƒ¨ç²’å­çš„ç‰¹æ€§ä»¥åŠè¿åŠ¨çŠ¶æ€çš„å®è§‚å‚é‡ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚ï¼šä½“ç³»çš„å‹åŠ›ã€‚

ç‰©æ€æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼šç³»ç»Ÿå¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€æ—¶ï¼Œå†…å‚é‡ä¾èµ–äºå¤–å‚é‡ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚æ°”ä½“å­˜åœ¨çš„å…³ç³»ï¼šf(p,â€†V,â€†T)â€„=â€„0ã€‚ç‰©è´¨åœ¨å…¶ä»–å½¢æ€ä¸‹çš„ç‰©æ€æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œåœ¨å·¥ç¨‹ç•Œæœ‰æ—¶å€™ä¹Ÿç§°ä¸ºæœ¬æ„æ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚

ç»Ÿè®¡åŠ›å­¦ä¸­ä½“ç³»åŠ›å­¦æè¿°çš„ä¸‰ç§ä¸åŒå±‚æ¬¡

Bogoliubovæå‡ºå…³äºç©ºé—´ã€æ—¶é—´ä¸Šå¤§è‡´æœ‰ä¸‰ç§ä¸åŒå°ºåº¦çš„æè¿°æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œåˆç§°ä¸ºä¸‰ç§æ ‡åº¦ã€‚ç²’å­é—´çš„ç›¸äº’ä½œç”¨åŠ›ç¨‹Lintï¼Œç²’å­å¹³å‡è‡ªç”±ç¨‹LÏ„å’Œä½“ç³»æ¸©åº¦ã€å¯†åº¦ç­‰éå‡åŒ€çš„é‡ç¨‹Lhã€‚

æè¿°å±‚æ¬¡ ç‰¹å¾é•¿åº¦ ç‰¹å¾æ—¶é—´ ä»¥å¸¸æ¸©ã€å¸¸å‹æ°¢æ°”ä¸ºä¾‹
å¾®è§‚å±‚æ¬¡ ç²’å­é—´ä½œç”¨åŠ›ç¨‹Lint ç›¸äº’ä½œç”¨æŒç»­æ—¶é—´Ï„int Lintâ€„=â€„10âˆ’8cm,â€†Ï„â€„=â€„5â€…Ã—â€…10âˆ’14s
åŠ¨ç†å­¦å±‚æ¬¡ ç²’å­å¹³å‡è‡ªç”±ç¨‹LÏ„ å¼›è±«æ—¶é—´Ï„ LÏ„â€„=â€„10âˆ’5cm,â€†Ï„â€„=â€„5â€…Ã—â€…10âˆ’11s
æµä½“åŠ›å­¦å±‚æ¬¡ éå‡åŒ€æ€§é‡ç¨‹Lh éå‡åŒ€æ€§ç‰¹å¾æ—¶é—´Ï„h Lhâ€„=â€„1cm,â€†Ï„hâ€„=â€„5â€…Ã—â€…10âˆ’6s

ç¬¬äºŒç« ï¼šç»å…¸åŠ¨åŠ›å­¦

Lagrangeå‡½æ•°

L(q,â€†qÌ‡,â€†t)â€„=â€„Tâ€…âˆ’â€…U

ä»¥ä¸‹è®¨è®ºä¿å®ˆåŠ›ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå³Fâ€„=â€„âˆ’âˆ‡Uï¼ŒLagrangeå‡½æ•°å¯ä»¥å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} L(q,\dot q)&=T(\dot q)-U(q)=\frac{1}{2}\sum_{i=1}^{3N} m_i \dot{x_i}^2-U \\ &= \frac{1}{2}\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\sum_{k,l=1}^{s^2} m_i \frac{\partial x_i}{\partial q_k}\frac{\partial x_i}{\partial q_l}\dot{q}_k\dot{q}_l-U(q) \\ &= \frac{1}{2}\sum_{k,l=1}^{s^2} M_{kl} \dot{q}_k\dot{q}_l-U(q) \\ \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­{x}ç§°ä¸ºdâ€™Alembertä½å½¢ï¼Œå¹¿ä¹‰è´¨é‡Nklå®šä¹‰ä¸ºï¼š $$M_{kl}= \sum_{i=1}^{3N}m_i\frac{\partial x_i}{\partial q_k}\frac{\partial x_i}{\partial q_l}$$

æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†å’Œlagrangeæ–¹ç¨‹

ä»æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†ï¼ˆHamiltonï¼‰å¯¼å‡ºLagrangeå½¢å¼çš„ç»å…¸åŠ›å­¦ã€‚åœ¨ç›¸ç©ºé—´ä¸­ï¼Œè®¾ä½“ç³»åœ¨t1æ—¶åˆ»ä»Aç‚¹å‡ºå‘ï¼Œç»è¿‡æŸè·¯å¾„q(t)åœ¨t2æ—¶åˆ»åˆ°è¾¾ç‚¹Bã€‚å¯¹äºæ¯æ¡å¯èƒ½çš„è·¯å¾„q(t)ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å®šä¹‰ä½œç”¨é‡ï¼ˆactionï¼‰ä¸ºï¼š

S[q(t)]â€„=â€„âˆ«t1t2L(qÌ‡,â€†q)ğ••t

å¯ä»¥çœ‹å‡ºä½œç”¨é‡æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ ‡é‡ï¼Œä¸ºè·¯å¾„çš„æ³›å‡½ã€‚

æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†åœ¨ç†è®ºä¸Šæœ‰å¾ˆå¤šæ¡è·¯å¾„å¯ä»¥å®ç°ä»Aç‚¹åˆ°Bç‚¹çš„ç›®çš„ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯å®é™…ä¸Šåªå­˜åœ¨ä¸€æ¡çœŸæ˜¯çš„è·¯å¾„ï¼Œè¿™æ¡è·¯å¾„åº”å½“æ»¡è¶³å¦‚ä¸‹è¦æ±‚ï¼š qtrueâ€„=â€„argminq{S[q(t)]}

ä»ç‰©ç†ä¸Šç†è§£ï¼Œå› ä¸ºä»Aåˆ°Béœ€è¦åœ¨ç›¸ç©ºé—´ä¸Šéœ€è¦æ»¡è¶³èƒ½é‡æœ€ä½åŸç†ã€‚å› æ­¤æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†æœ¬è´¨ä¸Šå°±æ˜¯æ»¡è¶³å‰è€…è¦æ±‚ã€‚

æ•…è€Œæ­¤é—®é¢˜æˆä¸ºä¸€ä¸ªæœ‰çº¦æŸçš„å˜åˆ†é—®é¢˜ã€‚è€ƒè™‘è·¯å¾„ä¸Šå¯èƒ½å­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªè™šä½ç§»q(t)â€„â†’â€„q(t)â€…+â€…Î´q(t)ï¼Œåœ¨Aã€Bä¸¤ç‚¹ç”±äºå›ºå®šçš„åŸå› ï¼Œä¸å­˜åœ¨è™šä½ç§»Î´q(tA)â€„=â€„Î´q(tB)â€„=â€„0ã€‚å¯¹ä½œç”¨é‡å…¬å¼è¿›è¡Œå˜åˆ†ï¼š

$$\begin{align} \delta S &=\int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\sum_{i=1}^{s}\{ \frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}\delta q_i+\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i}\delta \dot{q}_i\} \\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\sum_{i=1}^{s}\{ \frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}\delta q_i+\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i}\delta \frac{d q_i}{dt}\} \\ &= \delta\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i} \frac{d q_i}{dt}|_{t_1}^{t_2} + \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\sum_{i=1}^{s}\{ \frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}\delta q_i-\frac{d}{dt}\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i}\delta q_i \} \\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\sum_{i=1}^{s}\{ \frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}-\frac{d}{dt}\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i} \} \delta q_i\\ \end{align}$$

å¾—åˆ°æœ€ç»ˆçš„Lagrangeæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}-\frac{d}{dt}\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i}=0, \forall i=1,2,\cdots s$$

å¦‚æœå—åˆ°å¤–åŠ›fiextï¼Œåªéœ€è¦åœ¨å³è¾¹åŠ ä¸Šå¤–åŠ›é¡¹ï¼š $$\frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i}-\frac{d}{dt}\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot{q}_i}=f^{ext}_i, \forall i=1,2,\cdots s$$

Hamiltonæ­£åˆ™æ–¹ç¨‹

åˆ©ç”¨å‹’è®©å¾·å˜æ¢ï¼ˆLegendreï¼‰ï¼Œå°†ä¸€ç»„å˜é‡è½¬åŒ–ä¸ºå¦ä¸€ç»„å˜é‡ã€‚å°†L(qÌ‡,â€†q,â€†t)ä¸­çš„å˜é‡qÌ‡å˜ä¸º$p_i = \frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot q_i}$ï¼Œè®°pâ€„=â€„{pi}ï¼Œå®šä¹‰å“ˆå¯†é¡¿é‡ï¼ˆHamiltonianï¼‰ï¼š

$$\begin{equation}H(q,p,t)=\sum_{t=1}^{s}\dot q_ip_i - L(\dot q, q, t) \end{equation}$$

å­˜åœ¨ä»¥ä¸‹å…³ç³»ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{\partial H}{\partial t}&=\frac{\partial (\dot q_ip_i)}{\partial t} -\frac{\partial L}{\partial t} \\ &= -\frac{\partial L}{\partial t} \\ \frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i}&=-\frac{\partial L}{\partial q_i} \\ \frac{\partial H}{\partial \dot q_i}&=0 = p_i -\frac{\partial L}{\partial \dot q_i} \\ \frac{\partial H}{\partial p_i}&= \dot q_i\\ \end{align}$$

å°†å‰ä¸¤å¼ä»£å…¥Lagrangeæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{align} -\frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i}-\frac{d}{dt}p_i&=0, \forall i=1,2,\cdots s \\ \dot p_i &= -\frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i} \end{align}$$

å¾—åˆ°Hamiltonianæ­£åˆ™æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\begin{align} \dot p_i &= -\frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i} \\ \dot q_i &= \frac{\partial H}{\partial p_i} \end{align}$$

æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†ä¸Hamiltonæ­£åˆ™æ–¹ç¨‹

Hamiltonæ­£åˆ™æ–¹ç¨‹çš„å¯¼å‡ºï¼ŒåŒæ ·å¯ä»¥åˆ©ç”¨æœ€å°ä½œç”¨é‡åŸç†å¾—åˆ°ã€‚ç”±å¼ï¼ˆ7ï¼‰ã€ï¼ˆ8ï¼‰å’Œï¼ˆ13ï¼‰å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ï¼š

$$\begin{align} \delta S &= \delta\int_{t_1}^{t_2}L\mathbb{d}t \\ &= \delta\int_{t_1}^{t_2}(\sum_{i=1}^{s}\dot q_ip_i-H)\mathbb{d}t \\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\left( \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(\delta \dot q_ip_i+\dot q_i\delta p_i\right)-\delta H\right) \\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t\left( \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(\delta \dot q_ip_i+\dot q_i\delta p_i\right)-\left(\frac{\delta H}{\delta p}\delta p+\frac{\delta H}{\delta q}\delta q\right)\right) \\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(\delta \dot q_ip_i+\dot q_i\delta p_i-\frac{\delta H}{\delta p_i}\delta p_i-\frac{\delta H}{\delta q_i}\delta q_i\right)\\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(\delta \dot q_ip_i+\dot q_i\delta p_i-\dot q_i\delta p_i-\frac{\delta H}{\delta q_i}\delta q_i\right)\\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(\delta \dot q_ip_i-\frac{\delta H}{\delta q_i}\delta q_i\right)\\ &= \int_{t_1}^{t_2}\mathbb{d}t \sum_{i=1}^{s}\left(-\delta q_i\dot p_i-\frac{\delta H}{\delta q_i}\delta q_i\right)\\ \end{align}$$

æ ¹æ®Î´Sâ€„=â€„0å¯ä»¥å¾—å‡ºï¼š $$\dot p_i=-\frac{\delta H}{\delta q_i}$$

é’ˆå¯¹ä»¥ä¸Šæ¡ä»¶shannonè¯æ˜å”¯ä¸€è§£æ˜¯ï¼š $$H=-K\sum_{j=1}^{n}p_j\ln p_j$$ Kä¸ºä»»æ„å¸¸æ•°ã€‚

æ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°

å¯¹äºä¸‰ç»´ä½“ç³»ä¸­Nä¸ªç²’å­çš„ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå…¶ä½“ç³»ç›¸ç©ºé—´çš„ç›¸èƒä¸ºh3Nï¼Œå†å› ä¸ºæ˜¯å…¨åŒçš„ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªç›¸ä½“ç§¯å…ƒä»£è¡¨çš„å¾®è§‚ç²’å­æ•°ï¼š

$$\mathbb{d}\Gamma=\frac{dpdq}{h^{3N}N!}=\frac{1}{h^{3N}N!}\prod_{1}^{N}dp_i dq_i$$

è®¾tæ—¶åˆ»ä½“ç³»å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€åœ¨Î“ç›¸ç©ºé—´çš„ç›¸ä½“ç§¯å…ƒdÎ“ä¸­å‡ºç°çš„æ¦‚ç‡ä¸ºï¼š

dwâ€„=â€„f(q,â€†p,â€†t)dÎ“

å…¶ä¸­f(q,â€†p,â€†t)ç§°ä¸ºÎ“ç›¸ç©ºé—´ä½“ç³»çŠ¶æ€çš„æ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼Œä¹Ÿç§°ä¸ºç³»ç»¼åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°ï¼Œç®€ç§°åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°æˆ–è€…æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ã€‚

$$\begin{align} \int_{\Gamma}f(p,q,t)d\Gamma &= 1 \\ <A(t)>&=\int_{\Gamma}A(p,q)f(p,q,t)d\Gamma \end{align}$$

Liouvileæ–¹ç¨‹

Liouvileæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼šæ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦å‡½æ•°f(p,â€†q,â€†t)éšæ—¶é—´çš„å˜åŒ–è§„å¾‹ã€‚

ç›¸ç‚¹çš„é€Ÿåº¦ä¸º $$v=\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\dot q_i\hat{q}_i+\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\dot p_i\hat{p}_i$$ å…¶ä¸­qÌ‚,â€†pÌ‚æ˜¯æ–¹å‘å‘é‡ã€‚

å›ºå®šåŒºåŸŸVå†…çš„çŠ¶æ€ç‚¹çš„å¢é€Ÿï¼š $$\frac{\partial}{\partial t}\int_V f d\Gamma$$

ä»å›ºå®šåŒºåŸŸVä¸­æµå‡ºçš„çŠ¶æ€ç‚¹é€Ÿåº¦ï¼š âˆ®Sdsâ€…â‹…â€…vfâ€„=â€„âˆ«VdÎ“âˆ‡â€…â‹…â€…(fv) å…¶ä¸­dsæ˜¯è¡¨é¢å‘é‡ï¼Œè§„å®šæ–¹å‘ä¸ºå¤–æ³•å‘ã€‚

å› ä¸ºÎ“ç©ºé—´ä¸­ä¸å­˜åœ¨ç”ŸæˆçŠ¶æ€çš„æºï¼Œä¹Ÿä¸å­˜åœ¨æ¶ˆç­çŠ¶æ€çš„é»‘æ´ã€‚å› æ­¤åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªåŒºåŸŸä¸­ï¼Œæµå‡ºçš„çŠ¶æ€ä¸å¢åŠ çš„çŠ¶æ€åº”è¯¥æ˜¯ä¸€æ ·çš„ã€‚å› æ­¤å­˜åœ¨å…³ç³»ï¼š $$0=\frac{\partial}{\partial t}\int_V f d\Gamma+\int_V d\Gamma \nabla\cdot(fv)=\int_V d\Gamma\left(\frac{\partial f}{\partial t}+\nabla\cdot(fv)\right)$$

å¯¹äºä»»æ„åŒºåŸŸå‡æˆç«‹ï¼Œéœ€è¦æ»¡è¶³ï¼š $$\frac{\partial f}{\partial t}+\nabla\cdot(fv)=0$$

è€Œ$\frac{\partial f}{\partial t}=-\nabla\cdot(fv)=-\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{\partial (f\dot q_i)}{\partial q_i}+\frac{\partial (f\dot p_i)}{\partial p_i}\right)=-\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{\dot q_i\partial f}{\partial q_i}+\frac{f\partial \dot q_i}{\partial q_i}+\frac{\dot p_i\partial f}{\partial p_i}+\frac{f\partial \dot p_i}{\partial p_i}\right)=-\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{\dot q_i\partial f}{\partial q_i}+\frac{\dot p_i\partial f}{\partial p_i}\right)$å†æ ¹æ®Hamiltonæ­£åˆ™æ–¹ç¨‹å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ï¼š

$$\begin{align} \frac{\partial f}{\partial t} &= -\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{\dot q_i\partial f}{\partial q_i}+\frac{\dot p_i\partial f}{\partial p_i}\right) \\ &= -\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{ \partial f}{\partial q_i}\frac{\partial H}{\partial p_i}-\frac{\partial f}{\partial p_i}\frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i}\right) \\ &= \{H,f\} \end{align}$$

ä¸Šè¿°æ–¹ç¨‹ç§°ä¸ºLiouvileæ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚å…¶ä¸­Poissonæ‹¬å·å®šä¹‰ä¸º$\{A, B\}=\sum_{i=1}^{3N}\left(\frac{ \partial A}{\partial q_i}\frac{\partial B}{\partial p_i}-\frac{\partial A}{\partial p_i}\frac{\partial B}{\partial q_i}\right)$

ç»å…¸Liouvilleç®—ç¬¦çš„å½¢å¼è§£

å½¢å¼è§£å°±æ˜¯è§£æè§£ã€‚å¦‚æœç»å…¸Liouvilleç®—ç¬¦Lä¸æ—¶é—´æ— å…³ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”f(q,â€†p,â€†tâ€„=â€„0)å·²çŸ¥ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°$\frac{\partial f}{\partial t}|_{t=0}=(-iL)f|_{t=0}$ï¼Œé‡å¤è®¡ç®—âˆæ¬¡å¾—åˆ°$\frac{\partial^n f}{\partial t^n}|_{t=0}=(-iL)^n f|_{t=0}$ï¼Œæ¥ä¸‹æ¥å°†f(q,â€†p,â€†t)å±•å¼€ï¼š

$$\begin{align} f(q,p,t)&=\sum_{n=0}^{\infty}\frac{t^n}{n!}(\frac{\partial^n f}{\partial t^n})_{t=0} \\ &=\sum_{n=0}^{\infty}\frac{t^n}{n!}(-iL)^nf|_{t=0} \\ &= e^{-iLt}f(q,p,0) \end{align}$$

å› æ­¤ï¼š

f(q,â€†p,â€†t)â€„=â€„eâˆ’iLtf(q,â€†p,â€†0)

åŠ›å­¦é‡çš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–

ä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡Aâ€„=â€„A(q(t),â€†p(t),â€†t)çš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–å¯ä»¥å†™ä¸ºï¼š

$$\begin{align} \frac{d A}{dt}&=\frac{\partial A}{\partial t}+\sum_{i=1}^{3N}(\frac{\partial A}{\partial q_i}\dot q_i + \frac{\partial A}{\partial p_i}\dot p_i) \\ &= \frac{\partial A}{\partial t}+\sum_{i=1}^{3N}(\frac{\partial A}{\partial q_i}\frac{\partial H}{\partial p_i} + \frac{\partial A}{\partial p_i}\frac{\partial H}{\partial q_i}) \\ &= \frac{\partial A}{\partial t}+ \{A, H\} \\ &= \frac{\partial A}{\partial t}+ iLA \end{align}$$

ä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡çš„å¹³å‡å€¼

$$\begin{align} \frac{d \langle A\rangle}{dt}=\langle \frac{dA}{dt} \rangle \end{align}$$

ä¸æ˜¾å«æ—¶é—´çš„ç‰©ç†é‡

å¦‚æœAâ€„=â€„A(q(t),â€†p(t))é‚£ä¹ˆï¼š

$$\begin{align} \frac{d A}{d t}&=iLA \\ A(q(t), p(t)) &= e^{iLt}A(q(0),p(0)) \end{align}$$

ç»å…¸æ¼”åŒ–ç®—ç¬¦ã€æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°æ€§

é’ˆå¯¹ä¸‰ç»´Nç²’å­ä½“ç³»ï¼ŒHamiltonå†™ä¸ºï¼š

$$H(p,q)=\sum_{j=1}^{N} \frac{P_j^2}{2m_j}+U(q)$$

  1. Liouvilleç®—ç¬¦çš„Hermiteæ€§ Lâ€ â€„=â€„L
  2. å…¸å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€çš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–ã€‚

æ¼”åŒ–çŠ¶æ€çš„è§£æè§£ä¸ºï¼š x(t)â€„=â€„eiLtx(0) å…¶ä¸­ï¼Œå°†eiLtç§°ä¸ºç»å…¸ä¼ æ’­å­ï¼ˆclassical prograpatorï¼‰ï¼Œä¸é‡å­åŠ›å­¦ä¸­çš„eâˆ’iHt/â„ç›¸å¯¹åº”ã€‚ä¼ æ’­å­åˆç§°ä¸ºæ¼”åŒ–ç®—ç¬¦ã€‚

è®°æ¼”åŒ–ç®—ç¬¦U(t1,â€†t2)â€„=â€„U(t2â€…âˆ’â€…t1)â€„=â€„eiL(t2â€…âˆ’â€…t1)ï¼Œå³ï¼š U(t)â€„=â€„eiLt äºæ˜¯æœ‰x(t)â€„=â€„U(t)x(0)

  1. æ¼”åŒ–ç®—ç¬¦U(t)ä¸ºé…‰ç®—ç¬¦ã€‚ Uâ€ (t)U(t)â€„=â€„1

  2. æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°æ€§ã€‚

æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°ï¼šæ—¶é—´ä»0â€„â†’â€„tçš„æ¼”åŒ–è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼Œä¸æ—¶é—´ä»tâ€„â†’â€„0çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³ç›¸åŒçš„è¿åŠ¨æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºå…·æœ‰æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°æ€§ã€‚

Hamiltonæ–¹ç¨‹å…·æœ‰æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°æ€§ã€‚ä¼ æ’­å­ä¸æ—¶é—´åæ¼”å¯¹ç§°æ€§ç­‰ä»·ã€‚ è€ƒè™‘æ­£å‘è¿‡ç¨‹x(t)â€„=â€„U(t,â€†0)x(0)ï¼Œåœ¨è€ƒè™‘åå‘çš„ä¼ æ’­è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼š x(0)â€„=â€„U(0,â€†t)x(t)â€„=â€„U(âˆ’t)U(t)x(0)â€„=â€„Uâ€ (t)U(t)x(0)â€„=â€„x(0)

çº¦åŒ–åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°

å…¨åŒç²’å­ä½“ç³»çš„åŠ›å­¦é‡çš„å¹³å‡å€¼

âŸ¨B(t)âŸ©â€„=â€„âˆ«B(x1,â€†x2â‹¯xN)f(x1,â€†x2â‹¯xN)dx1dx2â‹¯dxN åœ¨å¤„ç†å…¨åŒä½“ç³»çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä»»æ„äº¤æ¢ä¸¤ä¸ªç²’å­çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä½“ç³»ä¸å˜ï¼Œå…·å¤‡å¦‚ä¸‹çš„æ¡ä»¶ï¼š

B(x1â‹¯xiâ‹¯xjâ‹¯xN)â€„=â€„B(x1â‹¯xjâ‹¯xiâ‹¯xN),â€†âˆ€iâ€„â‰ â€„j

è¿™ç§äº¤æ¢å¯¹ç§°æ€§å¯ä»¥å±•å¼€ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} B(x_1, x_2 \cdots x_N) = \sum_{n=0}^N B_n(x_1,x_2\cdots x_n) \end{equation}$$

å…¶ä¸­ï¼š $$\begin{align} B_0 &= b_0 \\ B_1 &= b_1(x_1)+b_1(x_2)+\cdots +b_1(x_N)=Nb_1(x) \\ B_2 &= b_2(x_1, x_2)+\cdots+b_2(x_1, x_N)+b_2(x_2, x_3)+\cdots+b_2(x_2, x_N)+\cdots+b_2(x_{N-1}, x_N) \\ &= C_N^2 b_2(x_1, x_2)=\frac{N!}{2!(N-1)!}b_2(x_1, x_2) \\ B_n &= \frac{N!}{n!(N-n)!}b_n(x_1,x_2\cdots x_n) \end{align}$$

b2(x1,â€†x2)æ˜¯ä¸èƒ½å†åˆ†è§£ä¸ºx1æˆ–è€…x2çš„å•å˜é‡å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç›´åˆ°ï¼Œbn(x1,â€†x2â‹¯xn)ä¸èƒ½å†åˆ†è§£ä¸ºæ›´å°‘å˜é‡çš„å‡½æ•°ã€‚é€šè¿‡ä»¥ä¸Šçš„æ„é€ ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç†è§£ä¸ºè½¬åŒ–ä¸ºä¸€ç§å…·å¤‡è½®æ¢å¯¹ç§°æ€§çš„åŸºåº•ï¼Œè¿›è¡Œå‡½æ•°çš„å±•å¼€ã€‚

åœ¨è®¡ç®—åŠ›å­¦é‡å¹³å‡å€¼çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle B(t)\rangle &= \sum_{n=0}^N \langle B_n(x_1,x_2\cdots x_n)\rangle \\ &= \sum_{n=0}^N \frac{N!}{n!(N-n)!}\langle b_n(x_1,x_2\cdots x_n)\rangle \\ &= \sum_{n=0}^N \frac{N!}{n!(N-n)!} \int b_n(x_1, x_2\cdots x_n)f_n(x_1, x_2\cdots x_n)dx_1 dx_2\cdots dx_n \end{align}$$

Bogoliubov-Born-Green-Kirkwood-Yvonçº§è”æ–¹ç¨‹

Liouvileæ–¹ç¨‹æ˜¯å…³äºNç²’å­çš„è¿åŠ¨æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œæ¶‰åŠ3Nâ€…+â€…1ä¸ªå˜é‡ï¼Œè•´å«çš„ä¿¡æ¯è¿œè¶…è¿‡å®è§‚è§‚æµ‹é‡éœ€è¦çš„ä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œæœ‰å¿…è¦è¿›è¡Œè¿›ä¸€æ­¥çš„æå–å…³é”®ä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œå³ä»åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°fçš„è§„å¾‹æ±‚å¯¼né˜¶çº¦åŒ–åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°çš„fnçš„è§„å¾‹ã€‚

HNä¸ºè¯¥Nç²’å­ä½“ç³»çš„Hamiltoné‡ï¼Œå³ï¼š $$\begin{align} H_N=\sum_{i=1}^{N}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ]+\sum_{i<j>}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j) \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­Vext(ri)ä¸ºç¬¬iä¸ªç²’å­å—åˆ°çš„å¤–åŠ¿ï¼ŒVijè¡¨ç¤ºå­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªä¸¤ä½“çš„ç›¸äº’ä½œç”¨ã€‚ä»¥ä¸‹å¯¼å‡ºné˜¶çº¦åŒ–åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°fnçš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–è§„å¾‹ã€‚

$$\begin{align} \frac{\partial f_n}{\partial t} &= \frac{\partial }{\partial t}\int f_N(x_1, x_2 \cdots x_N, t)d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \frac{\partial }{\partial t}f_N(x_1, x_2 \cdots x_N, t)d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ H_N, f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{N}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} +\int \left \{ \sum_{i<j}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹æœ‰$\sum_{i=1}^N(\cdot)=\sum_{i=1}^n(\cdot)+\sum_{i=n+1}^N(\cdot)$ï¼Œå°†ä¸Šå¼ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹è¿›è¡ŒåŒ–ç®€ï¼š $$\begin{align*} &\int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{N}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &=\int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ]+\sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \left \{ \left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \left \{ V_{ext}(r_i), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \left \{ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}, f_N\right \} d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \sum_{k=1}^{N} \left [ \nabla_{r_k} V_{ext}(r_i)\nabla_{p_k}f_N - \nabla_{p_k} V_{ext}(r_i)\nabla_{r_k}f_N\right ]d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \sum_{k=1}^{N}\left [ \nabla_{r_k}\frac{p_i^2}{2m}\nabla_{p_k}f_N-\nabla_{p_k}\frac{p_i^2}{2m}\nabla_{r_k}f_N\right ] d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \sum_{k=1}^{N}\left [ \nabla_{r_k} V_{ext}(r_i)\nabla_{p_k}f_N -\nabla_{p_k}\frac{p_i^2}{2m}\nabla_{r_k}f_N\right ] d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \sum_{i=n+1}^{N}\int \left [ \nabla_{r_i} V_{ext}(r_i)\nabla_{p_i}f_N -\frac{p_i}{m}\nabla_{r_i}f_N\right ] d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \text{ä½¿ç”¨Guasså…¬å¼æ¶ˆå»}\\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ \end{align*}$$

æ¥ä¸‹æ¥è®¨è®ºç¬¬äºŒé¡¹ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨$\sum_{i < j}^N(\cdot)=\sum_{i < j}^n(\cdot)+\sum_{i=1}^n\sum_{j=n+1}^{N}(\cdot)$ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆï¼š

$$\begin{align*} &\int \left \{ \sum_{i<j}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i<j}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\sum_{j=n+1}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i<j}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &+ \int \sum_{i=1}^{n}\sum_{j=n+1}^{N}\nabla_{r_i}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j)\cdot\nabla_{p_i}f_Nd x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ \end{align*}$$

æœ€åå¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{\partial f_n}{\partial t} &= \int \left \{ \sum_{i=1}^{n}\left [ \frac{p_i^2}{2m}+V_{ext}(r_i)\right ], f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} + \int \left \{ \sum_{i<j}^{N}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j), f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} + \int \sum_{i=1}^{n}\sum_{j=n+1}^{N}\nabla_{r_i}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j)\cdot\nabla_{p_i}f_Nd x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \int \left \{ H_n, f_N\right \}d x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} + \int \sum_{i=1}^{n}\sum_{j=n+1}^{N}\nabla_{r_i}V_{i j}(r_i,r_j)\cdot\nabla_{p_i}f_Nd x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \left \{ H_n, f_n\right \} + (N-n)\int \sum_{i=1}^{n}\nabla_{r_i}V_{i,j=(n+1)}\cdot\nabla_{p_i}f_Nd x_{n+1}dx_{n+2}\cdots dx_{N} \\ &= \left \{ H_n, f_n\right \} + (N-n)\int \sum_{i=1}^{n}\nabla_{r_i}V_{i,j=(n+1)}\cdot\nabla_{p_i}f_{n+1}dx_{n+1} \\ \end{align}$$

ä¸Šè¿°æ–¹ç¨‹ä¸ºçº§è”æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œå…¶å°†fnä¸fnâ€…+â€…1è”ç³»åœ¨ä¸€èµ·ã€‚

ä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡çš„âŸ¨B(q,â€†p)âŸ©çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡å€¼ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle B(q,p)\rangle=\int_{\tau}fB(q,p)dpdq=\lim_{\Delta E\to 0}C\int_{\Delta E} B(q,p)dqdp \end{align}$$

Poinacreå®šç†

Poinacreå›å½’å®šç†ï¼šå¯¹äºç­‰èƒ½é¢å†…çš„ä½“ç§¯æœ‰é™å¤§çš„å®è§‚ç³»ç»Ÿï¼Œå‡å®šå…¶Hamiltoné‡æœ‰ç•Œï¼Œåˆ™å…¶|p|,|q|å‡æœ‰ç•Œã€‚è‹¥æ—¶é—´tâ€„=â€„0æ—¶ï¼Œä½“ç³»ä»Ï„ç›¸ç©ºé—´çš„æŸç‚¹P0å‡ºå‘ï¼Œåˆ™ä½“ç³»åœ¨ä¸€æœ‰é™çš„æ—¶é—´Tå†…ï¼Œå¿…ç„¶ä¼šç»è¿‡P0ç‚¹è¶³å¤Ÿè¿‘çš„é‚»è¿‘ç‚¹Pâ€²0ï¼Œå…¶è·ç¦»å°äºä»»æ„å°çš„é¢„è®¾æ­£æ•°Ïµï¼Œå³|P0Pâ€²0|â€„<â€„Ïµã€‚

ç­‰æ¦‚ç‡åŸç†å’Œæœ€å¤§ç†µåŸç†

æœ¬èŠ‚ä¸»è¦è¯æ˜ï¼šæœ€å¤§ç†µåŸç†ç­‰ä»·äºå­¤ç«‹ç³»ç»Ÿè¾¾åˆ°å¹³è¡¡æ€åï¼Œä½“ç³»å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€åœ¨ç­‰èƒ½é¢ä¸Šå‘ˆç­‰æ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒçš„å‡è®¾ã€‚

æ—¶åˆ»tç³»ç»¼å¤„äºiæ€çš„æ ·æœ¬æ•°ç›®Niåœ¨dtæ—¶é—´ä¸­ï¼Œç¦»å¼€ä¸å¢åŠ çš„å˜åŒ–é‡ä»¥åŠå‡€å˜åŒ–é‡ï¼š $$\begin{align} (dN_i)_{-} &= \sum_{j(\neq i)}N_i P_{i\to j}dt \\ (dN_i)_{+} &= \sum_{j(\neq i)}N_j P_{j\to i}dt \\ dN_i &= (dN_i)_{+} - (dN_i)_{-} \\ &= \sum_{j(\neq i)}(N_j-N_i) P_{j\to i}dt \\ \frac{dN_i}{dt} &= \sum_{j(\neq i)}(N_j-N_i) P_{j\to i} \\ \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­Piâ€„â†’â€„jè¡¨ç¤ºä»iè·ƒè¿åˆ°jçš„æ¦‚ç‡ã€‚åŒæ ·å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{align} \dot p_i = \frac{dp_i}{dt} = \sum_{j(\neq i)}(p_j-p_i) P_{j\to i} \end{align}$$ æ ¹æ®ä¿¡æ¯ç†µçš„å®šä¹‰ï¼Œå®šä¹‰ä½“ç³»çš„é‡S:

$$\begin{align} S(t) &= -k_B\sum_i p_i(t)\ln p_i(t)=-k_B \langle \ln p_i(t) \rangle \\ \dot S &= -k_B\sum_i \dot p_iï¼ˆ\ln p_i+1ï¼‰\\ &=-k_B\sum_i \dot p_i\ln p_i \\ &= -k_B\sum_i \sum_{j(\neq i)}(p_j-p_i) P_{j\to i}\ln p_i \\ &= -k_B\sum_i \sum_{j}(p_j-p_i) \ln p_i P_{j\to i}\\ &= \frac{-k_B}{2}\sum_i \sum_{j} \left [ (p_j-p_i) \ln p_i P_{j\to i} +(p_i-p_j) \ln p_j P_{i\to j}\right ]\\ &= \frac{k_B}{2}\sum_i \sum_{j} (p_i-p_j) (\ln p_i -\ln p_j)P_{i\to j}\\ \end{align}$$

å› ä¸ºPiâ€„â†’â€„jâ€„>â€„0ï¼Œå¯çŸ¥SÌ‡â€„>â€„0ï¼ŒSæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ’å¢çš„é‡ã€‚å½“ä»»æ„çš„è·ƒè¿é‡ä¹‹é—´æ»¡è¶³: $$\begin{align} p_i=p_j=\cdots=\frac{1}{\Omega} \end{align}$$ å°±ä¼šæœ‰SÌ‡â€„=â€„0ï¼Œè¾¾åˆ°æœ€ç»ˆçš„å¹³è¡¡æ€ã€‚å³å¾—åˆ°Sçš„æœ€å¤§å€¼ï¼ŒGibbsç†µï¼š $$\begin{align} S=k_B \ln \Omega \end{align}$$

æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼

æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼ï¼šä½“ç§¯Vã€ç²’å­æ•°Nå’Œæ¸©åº¦Tæ’å®šçš„ä½“ç³»ï¼Œä¹Ÿç§°ä¸º(N,â€†V,â€†T)ä½“ç³»ã€‚

è®¾{Hi}ä¸ºä½“ç³»çš„Hamiltoné‡ï¼Œå¯¹æ‰€æœ‰æ ·æœ¬æ±‚å’Œå¾—åˆ°ç³»ç»¼çš„Hamiltoné‡Hensï¼š $$\begin{align} H_{ens}=\sum_{i=1}^{N}H_i+\text{çƒ­äº¤æ¢é¡¹} \end{align}$$

å½“ä½“ç³»ç²’å­æ•°ä¸å¤ªå°‘ï¼Œçƒ­äº¤æ¢é¡¹å¯ä»¥å°åˆ°å¿½ç•¥ã€‚è®¾æ ·æœ¬çš„ä½“ç³»ç¬¬jç§çŠ¶æ€çš„èƒ½é‡ä¸ºEjï¼Œåˆè®¾ç³»ç»¼ä¸­åŒå±äºç¬¬jç§çŠ¶æ€çš„æ ·æœ¬ä½“ç³»æ•°ä¸ºnjã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œå¯¹æ‰€æœ‰ä½“ç³»çŠ¶æ€æ±‚å’Œå¾—åˆ°ç³»ç»¼çš„æ€»èƒ½é‡ï¼š $$\begin{align} \epsilon=\sum_{j}^{\text{state}}n_j E_j \end{align}$$

å› ä¸ºæ•´ä¸ªæ­£åˆ™ä½“ç³»æ˜¯å­¤ç«‹çš„ï¼Œå› æ­¤ç³»ç»¼çš„èƒ½é‡Ïµæ˜¯ä¸å˜çš„ã€‚åˆå¯¹æ‰€æœ‰çš„ä½“ç³»çŠ¶æ€njæ±‚å’Œï¼Œå¾—åˆ°ç³»ç»¼ä¸­çš„æ ·æœ¬æ ·æœ¬ä½“ç³»æ€»æ•°Nï¼Œå³ï¼š $$\begin{align} N=\sum_j^{\text{state}}n_j \end{align}$$

æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼çš„æœ€å¯å‡ åˆ†å¸ƒ

åœ¨ç»™å®šæ ·æœ¬æ€»æ•°Nå’Œç³»ç»¼èƒ½é‡Ïµçš„çº¦æŸæ¡ä»¶ä¸‹ï¼Œå¯»æ‰¾åˆ†å¸ƒ{nj}å¯ä»¥ä½¿å¾—æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼çš„å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€Wè¾¾åˆ°æœ€å¤§ã€‚æŒ‰ç…§æ’åˆ—ç»„åˆçš„åŸç†ï¼Œç»™å®šåˆ†å¸ƒ{nj}ï¼ŒNä¸ªæ ·æœ¬æ„æˆçš„æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼çš„å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€æ•°ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} W=\frac{N!}{\prod_j n_j !} \end{align}$$

æœ¬è´¨æ˜¯è§£å†³ä¸€ä¸ªå˜åˆ†é—®é¢˜ï¼Œåœ¨æ»¡è¶³èƒ½é‡ä¸æ ·æœ¬æ•°çº¦æŸçš„æ¡ä»¶ä¸‹ï¼Œå¯»æ‰¾{ni}åˆ†å¸ƒï¼Œä½¿å¾—Wæœ€å¤§ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \Omega = \ln W-\alpha (\sum_j n_j-N)-\beta (\sum_j n_j E_j-\epsilon) \end{align}$$

åˆ©ç”¨Lagrangeä¹˜å­æ³•ï¼Œæå€¼æ—¶åº”æ»¡è¶³ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{\delta \Omega}{\delta n_j}&=0,\forall j \\ \ln W &= \ln \left (\frac{N!}{\prod_j n_j !}\right) \\ &\simeq N\ln N-N-\sum_j (n_j\ln n_j-n_j) \\ \frac{\partial \ln W}{\partial n_j} &= -\ln n_j \\ \frac{\delta \Omega}{\delta n_j}&= -\ln n_j-\alpha-\beta E_j =0 \\ n_j^* &= e^{-\alpha-\beta E_j} \\ \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­nj*è¡¨ç¤ºæœ€å¯å‡ åˆ†å¸ƒã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œä½“ç³»å¤„äºç¬¬jä¸ªæ€çš„æ¦‚ç‡ä¸ºï¼š

$$\begin{align} P_j &= \frac{n_j}{N} = \frac{e^{-\alpha-\beta E_j}}{\sum_i^{\text{state}}e^{-\alpha-\beta E_i}} \\ &= \frac{e^{-\beta E_j}}{\sum_i^{\text{state}}e^{-\beta E_i}} \\ &= \frac{e^{-\beta E_j}}{Z} \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­Zæ˜¯é…åˆ†å‡½æ•°ã€‚ å…·ä½“çš„ç‰©ç†é‡è®¡ç®—å¯ä»¥å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle B\rangle = \sum_j P_j B_j = \frac{1}{Z}\sum_j B_j e^{-\beta E_j} \end{align}$$

æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼ä¸­çš„çƒ­åŠ›å­¦å…³ç³»

  1. ä½“ç³»å¹³å‡èƒ½é‡ $$\begin{align} \langle E\rangle = \frac{1}{Z}\sum_j E_j e^{-\beta E_j} = -\left(\frac{\partial \ln Z}{\partial \beta}\right)_{N,V} \end{align}$$
  2. Helmholtzè‡ªç”±èƒ½ $$\begin{align} \langle F\rangle = -\frac{1}{\beta}\ln Z \end{align}$$
  3. å¹³å‡å‹å¼º $$\begin{align} \langle p\rangle = \frac{1}{\beta}\left(\frac{\partial \ln Z}{\partial V}\right)_{N,T} \end{align}$$
  4. ç†µçš„æœŸæœ›å€¼ $$\begin{align} \langle S\rangle &= \frac{\langle E\rangle}{Z}+k_B\ln Z = \frac{1}{\beta}\left(\frac{\partial \ln Z}{\partial T}\right)_{N,V} + k_B\ln Z \\ &= k_B \left [\frac{\partial (T\ln Z)}{\partial T}\right]_{N,V} \end{align}$$
  5. æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼çš„å¾®è§‚çŠ¶æ€æ•° $$\begin{align} W^* &=\frac{N!}{\prod_j n_j^* !}= Z^N e^{-\beta \epsilon} \end{align}$$
  6. åŒ–å­¦åŠ¿ $$\begin{align} \mu = \frac{-1}{\beta}\left(\frac{\partial \ln Z}{\partial N}\right)_{V,T} \end{align} $$

å·¨æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼

å·¨æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼ï¼šä½“ç§¯Vå›ºå®šï¼Œä¸ç¯å¢ƒå­˜åœ¨èƒ½é‡ä¸ç²’å­æ•°äº¤æ¢ã€‚ä½“ç³»çš„ä¸å˜é‡ä¸ºä½“ç§¯Vã€æ¸©åº¦Tã€åŒ–å­¦åŠ¿Î¼ã€‚

è®¾H(N)ä¸ºè¯¥ç²’å­æ•°Nçš„ä½“ç³»çš„Hamiltoné‡ï¼Œ|N,â€†jâŸ©ä¸ºè¯¥ä½“ç³»ç¬¬jä¸ªæœ¬å¾æ€ï¼Œå¯¹åº”çš„èƒ½é‡ä¸ºEN,â€†jï¼Œå­˜åœ¨ï¼š $$\begin{align} H(N)|N,j\rangle = |N,j\rangle E_{N,j} \end{align}$$

è®¾{Hi}ä¸ºæ ·æœ¬ä½“ç³»çš„Hamiltoné‡ï¼Œå¯¹æ‰€æœ‰æ ·æœ¬æ±‚å’Œå¾—åˆ°ç³»ç»¼çš„Hamiltoné‡HGCEä¸ºï¼š

ä½“ç³»å¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼Œç‰©ç†é‡çš„æ¶¨è½ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \Delta A(r) \equiv A(r) - \langle A(r) \rangle \end{align}$$ æ˜¾ç„¶å¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€çš„ä½“ç³»æ¶¨è½ä¸ºé›¶ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle \Delta A(r) \rangle = \langle A(r) - \langle A(r) \rangle \rangle = 0 \end{align}$$ ä½†æ˜¯æ¶¨è½å¹³æ–¹çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡å€¼å…·æœ‰ç¡®å®šæ•°å€¼ï¼Œè®¾ä¸ºaï¼Œå³ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle (\Delta A(r))^2 \rangle = \langle [A(r) - \langle A(r) \rangle]^2 \rangle = a \end{align}$$ å‡å®šä¸å­˜åœ¨å¤–åœºï¼Œåˆ™å¤„äºå¹³è¡¡æ€çš„ä½“ç³»åº”å½“æ˜¯å‡åŒ€çš„ï¼Œäºæ˜¯aä¸ä½ç½®æ— å…³ã€‚

å¯¹äºä½“ç³»å†…çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªç©ºé—´ä½ç½®rä¸râ€²ï¼Œä½ç½®rå¤„çš„ç‰©ç†é‡A(r)å’Œå¦ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®râ€²å¤„çš„å¦ä¸€ä¸ªç‰©ç†é‡B(râ€²)çš„ä¹˜ç§¯çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡å€¼ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle A(r) B(r')\rangle \equiv C_{AB}(r,r') \end{align}$$ ç§°ä¸ºè¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªé‡çš„ç©ºé—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ï¼Œæè¿°ä¸åŒä½ç½®ä¸Šçš„ä¸¤ä¸ªç‰©ç†é‡ä¹‹é—´çš„è”ç³»ï¼Œâ€œä¹˜ç§¯â€åæ˜ æŸç§å¹³å‡åŒ–åçš„ç‰¹å¾ã€‚ å…¶ä¸­ä¸€ä¸ªç‰¹ä¾‹ï¼Œå¦‚æœæè¿°çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªç‰©ç†é‡ç›¸åŒï¼Œç§°ä¹‹ä¸ºç©ºé—´çš„è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle A(r) A(r')\rangle \equiv C_{AA}(r,r') \end{align}$$

å¯¹äºå¹³è¡¡æ€æ¥è¯´ï¼Œå› ä¸ºå…·æœ‰å‡åŒ€æ€§ï¼Œç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°çš„ç»å¯¹ä½ç½®æ˜¯ä¸é‡è¦çš„ï¼Œé‡è¦çš„æ˜¯ç›¸å¯¹ä½ç½®ï¼ˆå…·æœ‰ç©ºé—´ä½ç½®å¹³ç§»ä¸å˜æ€§ï¼‰ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle A(r)B(r')\rangle = \langle A(r-r')B(0) \rangle \end{align}$$

è¿›ä¸€æ­¥ï¼Œå¦‚æœä½“ç³»æ˜¯å„å‘åŒæ€§ï¼Œåˆ™ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ä¸ä½ç½®å‘é‡æ— å…³ï¼Œä»…ä¸ä¸¤ç‚¹é—´è·|râ€…âˆ’â€…râ€²|æœ‰å…³ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬æ¥è¯´ï¼Œåœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªè·ç¦»Î¾å†…ï¼Œç©ºé—´ç›¸å…³æ€§CABå€¼ä¸å°ï¼Œè€Œå¤§äºÎ¾ä¹‹åç›¸å…³æ€§å˜å¾—å¾ˆå°ï¼Œåˆ™é•¿åº¦Î¾å¯ä½œä¸ºç©ºé—´ç›¸èŒƒå›´çš„åº¦é‡ï¼Œç§°ä¹‹ä¸ºç›¸å…³é•¿åº¦ã€‚

ä½ç½®çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ã€åŠ¨é‡çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦

Nä¸ªå…¨åŒç²’å­ä½“ç³»çš„ä¿„æ•°å¯†åº¦Ï(r)æŒ‡ä½ç½®rå¤„å•ä½ä½“ç§¯ä¸­çš„ç²’å­ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œå³Ï(r)drä¸ºä½“ç§¯å…ƒdrä¸­çš„ç²’å­ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œç»å…¸åŠ›å­¦æ„ä¹‰ä¸Šå¯ä»¥è¡¨ç¤ºä¸ºï¼š $$\rho(r)=\sum_{i=1}^N\delta(r-r_i)$$

ä½“ç³»æ•°å¯†åº¦Ï(r)çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡å€¼ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle \rho(r)\rangle &= \int dr\rho(r)f_N(r_1\cdots r_N)=\int dr \sum_{i=1}^N\delta(r-r_i)f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ &= N\int dr_1 \delta(r-r_i) \int dr_2\cdots r_N f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ \end{align}$$ å¼•å…¥å®šä¹‰ï¼š f1(r1)â€„â‰¡â€„Vâˆ«dr2â‹¯rNfN(r1â‹¯rN) å¯å¾—ï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle \rho(r)\rangle &= N \int dr_1\delta(r-r_1)\frac{1}{V}f_1(r_1)=\frac{N}{V}f_1(r) \\ &= \rho f_1(r) \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­f1(r)çš„ç‰©ç†å«ä¹‰ä¸ºï¼›ä¸ç®¡å…¶å®ƒç²’å­çš„åˆ†å¸ƒæƒ…å†µï¼Œæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªç²’å­å‡ºç°åœ¨rå¤„çš„æ¦‚ç‡å†ä¹˜ä»¥ä½“ç§¯ã€‚å¯¹äºå‡åŒ€ä½“ç³»ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªæ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒæ˜¾ç„¶ä¸ä½ç½®æ— å…³å¹¶ä¸”ç­‰äº$\frac{1}{V}$ï¼Œå³å¯¹äºå‡åŒ€ç³»ï¼š $$\begin{align*} \int d_2\cdots d_N f_N(r_1\cdots r_N)&=\frac{1}{V} \\ f_1(r) &= 1 \end{align*}$$

æ¥ä¸‹æ¥è®¨è®ºæ•°å¯†åº¦çš„ç©ºé—´ç›¸å…³æ€§ã€‚ $$\begin{align} \langle \rho(r)\rho(r')\rangle &= \int dr \rho(r)\rho (r') f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ &= \int dr_1\cdots dr_N \sum_{i=1}^N\sum_{j=1}^N\delta(r-r_i)\delta(r'-r_j)f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ &= \int dr_1\cdots dr_N \left[ \sum_{i=1}^N\delta(r-r_i)\delta(r'-r_i)+\sum_{i\neq j}\delta(r-r_i)\delta(r-r_j)\right]f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ &= \rho \delta(r-r')+N(N-1)\int dr_1 dr_2 \delta(r-r_1)\delta(r'-r_2) \int dr_3\cdots dr_N f_N(r_1\cdots r_N) \\ &= \rho \delta(r-r')+\frac{N(N-1)}{V^2}\int dr_1 dr_2 \delta(r-r_1)\delta(r'-r_2) f_2(r_1, r_2) \\ &= \rho \delta(r-r') + \rho^2 f_2(r_1, r_2) \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰f2ä¸ºï¼š f2(r1,â€†r2)â€„â‰¡â€„V2âˆ«dr3â‹¯drNfN(r1â‹¯rN)

æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»¼ä¸­çš„ç©ºé—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°

æ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°è¡¨è¿°ç‰©è´¨è¿åŠ¨åœ¨æ—¶é—´å…ˆåä¸Šçš„ç›¸å…³å…³ç³»ï¼Œå…·å¤‡å¦‚ä¸‹çš„æ€§è´¨ï¼š 1. ç”±äºäººä¸€ç‰©ç†é‡åœ¨æœ¬è´¨ä¸Šå¿…é¡»æ˜¯å®æ•°ï¼Œå› æ­¤æ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°å¿…é¡»æ˜¯å®æ•°ã€‚ 2. limtâ€„â†’â€„âˆâŸ¨B(0)C(0)âŸ©â€„=â€„0ï¼Œä¸¤ä¸ªæ—¶é—´é—´éš”æ— ç©·è¿œçš„äº‹ä»¶è‡ªç„¶ä¸ç›¸å…³äº†ã€‚ è¡¨ç¤ºæ€€ç–‘ï¼ŒçœŸçš„æ˜¯è¿™æ ·ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ

å¹³è¡¡æ€æ—¶é—´è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°çš„æ€§è´¨

å¹³è¡¡æ€æ—¶çš„æ—¶é—´è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•° âŸ¨CBB(t1,â€†t2)â€„â‰¡â€„âŸ¨B(t1)B(t2)âŸ©ï¼Œå…·æœ‰å¦‚ä¸‹æ€§è´¨ï¼š 1. æ—¶é—´å¹³ç§»ä¸å˜æ€§ã€‚è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°åªä¸æ—¶é—´é—´éš”Ï„â€„â‰¡â€„t1â€…âˆ’â€…t2æœ‰å…³: $$\begin{align*} C_{BB}(t_1, t_2) &\equiv \langle B(t_1)B(t_2)\rangle = \langle B(0)B(t_2-t_1)\rangle \\ &= \rangle = \langle B(0)B(\tau)\rangle \equiv C_{BB}(\tau) \end{align*}$$ 2. æ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°çš„åº”ç”¨

é‡å­åŠ¨åŠ›å­¦

è¿ç»­ä»‹è´¨åŠ›å­¦

éå¹³è¡¡æ€ç»Ÿè®¡åŠ›å­¦åˆ†ä¸ºå¤šç§å½¢å¼ç†è®ºï¼š * å¾®è§‚å±‚æ¬¡ * åŠ¨ç†å­¦å±‚æ¬¡ * æµä½“åŠ›å­¦å±‚æ¬¡ ä»¥ä¸Šä¸‰ä¸ªå±‚æ¬¡ï¼Œé€æ¸ç²—ç²’åŒ–ã€‚åœ¨æµä½“åŠ›å­¦å±‚æ¬¡ï¼Œå…ˆå°†å¤„ç†çš„ä½“ç³»è®¾æƒ³ä¸ºè¿ç»­ä»‹è´¨ï¼Œç„¶åç”¨è¿ç»­ä»‹è´¨æ¥ç ”ç©¶è¿™ä¸€å±‚æ¬¡çš„é—®é¢˜ã€‚

åŸºæœ¬æ¦‚å¿µ

å‹å¼ºå¼ é‡å’Œåº”åŠ›å¼ é‡

ç²˜æ€§æ¶²ä½“æˆ–è€…å›ºä½“ä¸­ä»»æ„å•ä½æˆªé¢ä¸Šå—åˆ°çš„åŠ›ä¸ä¸€å®šåœ¨è¯¥æˆªé¢çš„æ³•å‘ä¸Šï¼Œéœ€è¦æ‹“å±•ä¸ºå¼ é‡åˆ©ç”¨9ä¸ªæ ‡é‡æè¿°ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºå‹å¼ºå¼ é‡Pâ€„â‰¡â€„{pÎ±Î²|Î±,â€†Î²â€„=â€„x,â€†y,â€†z}ï¼Œåœ¨ç›´è§’åæ ‡ç³»ä¸‹å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} P= \begin{bmatrix} p_{xx} & p_{xy} & p_{xz}\\ p_{yx} & p_{yy} & p_{yz}\\ p_{zx} & p_{zy} & p_{zz}\\ \end{bmatrix} \end{align}$$

åº”åŠ›å¼ é‡Ïƒå–åæ–¹å‘ï¼šÏƒâ€„â‰¡â€„âˆ’Pï¼Œå®šä¹‰æ³•å‘é‡$\bf n$ï¼Œè¯¥ç•Œé¢ä¸Šé¢çš„åŠ›$\bf\sigma_n$ä¸ºï¼š $$\bf{\sigma_n} =\sigma \cdot \bf n$$ åŒæ—¶ï¼Œåº”åŠ›å¼ é‡ä¸ºï¼š

$$\sigma = \sum_{i,j=1}^3\sigma_{ij}e_ie_j \triangleq \sigma_{ij}e_ie_j$$

å…¶ä¸­â‰œæ˜¯Einsteinæ±‚å’Œç¬¦å·ã€‚

åº”å˜å¼ é‡

ä»¥ä¸‹è®¨è®ºç‰©ä½“å—åŠ›åä½“å†…ç²’å­ä½ç½®å‘ç”Ÿçš„ç›¸å¯¹æ”¹å˜ã€‚

ä½“å†…æ— é™æ¥è¿‘çš„ä¸¤ç‚¹Pâ€Šâ€Qï¼Œå½¢å˜å‰å‘é‡$\overrightarrow{PQ}\equiv dr = \sum_{i=1}^3dx_ie_i$ï¼Œå½¢å˜åæˆä¸ºå‘é‡$\overrightarrow{P'Q'}\equiv dr'=dr+du = \sum_{i=1}^3(dx_i+du_i)e_i$ï¼Œä½ç§»å˜é‡duâ€„=â€„drâ€²â€…âˆ’â€…drã€‚

$$\begin{align} |dr'|^2 &= \sum_{i=1}^3(dx_i+du_i)^2 = \sum_{i=1}^3(dx_i+\sum_{k=1}^3\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}dx_k)^2 \\ &= \sum_{i=1}^3 \left[ (dx_i)^2 +2dx_i\sum_{k=1}^3\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}dx_k+\left(\sum_{k=1}^3\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}dx_k\right)^2\right] \\ &= |dr|^2 + 2\sum_{i=1}^3dx_i \sum_{k=1}^3\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}dx_k + \sum_{i,k,l=1}^3\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_l}dx_kdx_l \\ &= |dr|^2 + 2\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}dx_kdx_i + \frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_l}dx_kdx_l \\ &= |dr|^2 + \left(\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}+\frac{\partial u_k}{\partial x_i}+\frac{\partial u_l}{\partial x_l}\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_i}\right) dx_kdx_l \\ &= |dr|^2 + 2\epsilon_{ij} dx_kdx_l \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­ä»¤ï¼š $$\epsilon_{ij}\equiv \left(\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}+\frac{\partial u_k}{\partial x_i}+\frac{\partial u_l}{\partial x_l}\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_i}\right)$$

å¯¹è§’å…ƒç§°ä¸ºæ­£å‘åº”å˜ï¼Œéå¯¹è§’å…ƒç§°ä¸ºåˆ‡å‘åº”å˜æˆ–è€…å‰ªåº”å˜ã€‚åœ¨åº”å˜æ¯”è¾ƒå°çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼ŒäºŒé˜¶å¾®åˆ†é¡¹è¿œå°äºä¸€é˜¶ç›¸ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¿½ç•¥ã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼š $$\begin{align} \epsilon_{ij} &\approx \left(\frac{\partial u_i}{\partial x_k}+\frac{\partial u_k}{\partial x_i}\right) \\ \epsilon &= \frac{1}{2}\left[\nabla u+\nabla u^T\right] \end{align}$$

å¹¿ä¹‰Hookeå®šå¾‹

åœ¨è¿ç»­å½¢å˜ä¹‹åï¼Œåº”åŠ›å¼ é‡Ïƒå¯æ™®ä¸–çš„è®¤ä¸ºæ˜¯åº”å˜å¼ é‡çš„ä¿„Ïµå‡½æ•°ï¼Œå³Ïƒ(Ïµ)ã€‚åœ¨æ— åˆåº”åŠ›ä¸”åº”å˜è¾ƒå°çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œç•¥å»é«˜æ¬¡é¡¹å¾—ï¼š $$\sigma_{ij}=\left( \frac{\partial \sigma_{ij}}{\partial \epsilon_{kl}}\right)_0\epsilon_{kl}$$

å…¶ä¸­ä¸‹æ ‡ä¸º0è¡¨ç¤ºåœ¨åº”å˜ä¸º0å¤„å–å€¼ã€‚

å½“å½¢å˜è¾ƒå°çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œé¥°æ¼”çš„åº”åŠ›ä¸åº”å˜å€¼ä¹‹é—´æœä»Hookeå®šå¾‹ï¼Œå°†åå¾®åˆ†å…³ç³»å˜ä¸ºçº¿æ€§å…³ç³»ï¼š Ïƒijâ€„=â€„CijklÏµlk

å½¢å˜èƒ½

å„é¡¹åŒæ€§ä»‹è´¨çš„å½¢å˜èƒ½

å„é¡¹åŒæ€§ä»‹è´¨çš„åº”åŠ›å¼ é‡

æµä½“åŠ›å­¦

æµä½“åŠ›å­¦å°±æ˜¯è¿ç»­ä»‹è´¨åŠ›å­¦ã€‚Newtonç²˜æ€§å…¬å¼ï¼Œå‰ªåˆ‡åº”åŠ›$\tau\equiv \frac{f}{\delta S}$æ­£æ¯”äºåˆ‡å‘é€Ÿåº¦ï¼š $$\tau=\eta \frac{dv}{dy}$$

æµä½“çš„è¿åŠ¨æ–¹ç¨‹

æµä½“çš„è¿ç»­æ€§æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š

$$\begin{align} \frac{\partial \rho_m}{\partial t}+\nabla\cdot \bf j &=0 \\ \bf{j}(r,t) &= \rho_m \bf m \\ \end{align}$$

ç†æƒ³æµä½“çš„è¿åŠ¨æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\rho_m \frac{Dv}{Dt}=\rho_m(\frac{v}{t}-v\cdot\nabla v)=-\nabla\cdot P$$

éå¹³è¡¡çƒ­åŠ›å­¦åŸºç¡€

å› ä¸ºâ€„<â€„Î”Bâ€„>â€„â€„=â€„0æ’æˆç«‹ï¼Œä¸ºäº†è¡¨å¾æ¶¨è½çš„ç¨‹åº¦ï¼Œéœ€å°†åå·®çš„å¹³æ–¹å¯¹é‡å­æ€æ±‚å¹³å‡å€¼ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºBåœ¨ç³»ç»¼ä¸­çš„å‡æ–¹æ¶¨è½ï¼Œç®€ç§°æ¶¨è½ï¼š $$\begin{align} <(\Delta B)^2> &\equiv \sum_j P_j - (\Delta B)^2 =\left < (B-<\Delta B>)^2\right> \\ &= \sum_j P_j\left(B_j-\langle B\rangle\right)^2=\sum_j P_j B_j^2-2 \sum_j P_j B_j\langle B\rangle+\sum_j P_j\langle B\rangle^2 \\ &= \langle B^2\rangle -\langle B\rangle^2 \end{align}$$

å…¶ä¸­âŸ¨B2âŸ©ä¸ºç‰©ç†é‡B2çš„å‡å€¼ï¼Œæˆ–Bçš„å‡æ–¹å€¼ã€‚åŒæ ·ï¼Œç›¸å¯¹åå·®å¹³æ–¹çš„å‡å€¼å¯è¡¨ä¸ºï¼š

ç§°ä¸ºçƒ­åŠ›å­¦é‡Bçš„ç›¸å¯¹æ¶¨è½ã€‚

åœ¨è¿ç»­è°±æ—¶å€™çš„æƒ…å†µ

æ ¹æ®$\langle E\rangle=k_B T^2\left( \frac{\partial \ln Z}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N}$å¾—åˆ°$\left( \frac{\partial Z}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N}=\frac{Z}{k_B T^2}\langle E\rangle$ï¼Œå› æ­¤ï¼š $$\begin{align} \left(\frac{\partial\langle E\rangle}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N} = \frac{1}{k_B T^2}\left[\langle E^2\rangle-\langle E\rangle^2\right] \end{align}$$

æ ¹æ®å®šå®¹çƒ­å®¹$C_V = \left(\frac{\partial\langle E\rangle}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N}$ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°æ­£åˆ™ç³»ç»Ÿçš„èƒ½é‡æ¶¨è½å’Œèƒ½é‡çš„ç›¸å¯¹æ¶¨è½åˆ†åˆ«ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{gathered} \left\langle(\Delta E)^2\right\rangle=\left\langle E^2\right\rangle-\langle E\rangle^2=k_{\mathrm{B}} T^2\left(\frac{\partial\langle E\rangle}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N}=k_{\mathrm{B}} T^2 C_V \\ \left\langle r_E^2\right\rangle=\frac{\left\langle(\Delta E)^2\right\rangle}{\langle E\rangle^2}=\frac{1}{\langle E\rangle^2} k_{\mathrm{B}} T^2\left(\frac{\partial\langle E\rangle}{\partial T}\right)_{V, N}=k_{\mathrm{B}} T^2 \frac{C_V}{\langle E\rangle^2} \propto \frac{1}{N} \end{gathered} \end{equation}$$

Onsageræ¶¨è½å›å½’å‡è®¾çš„æ•°å­¦æè¿°

åŸºäºä¸Šè¿°å¯¹äºå¹³è¡¡æ¶¨è½çš„æ—¶é—´è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç°åœ¨è€ƒè™‘éå¹³è¡¡ä½“ç³»å¼€å§‹ç›¸å¹³è¡¡çš„å¼›è±«ã€‚è®¾tâ€„=â€„0æ—¶æ’¤åŒºå¤–åœºè®©åˆ¶å¤‡å¾—åˆ°çš„éå¹³è¡¡ä½“ç³»å¼€å§‹ç›¸å¹³è¡¡æ€ä½œè‡ªç”±å¼›è±«ã€‚Onsageræ¶¨è½å›å½’å‡è®¾æ˜¯æŒ‡åœ¨çº¿æ€§èŒƒå›´å†…ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å‡è®¾å¼›è±«æœä»å¦‚ä¸‹æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{\Delta \bar A(t)}{\Delta\bar A(0)}=\frac{C(t)}{C(0)} \end{align}$$ å·¦è¾¹è¡¨ç¤ºéå¹³è¡¡ä½“ç³»å‘å¹³è¡¡æ€ä½œå®è§‚å¼›è±«çš„è¡°å‡ç¨‹åº¦ï¼Œå³è¾¹è¡¨ç¤ºå¹³è¡¡æ¶¨è½çš„è‡ªç›¸å…³è¡Œä¸ºæˆ–å¾®è§‚å¼›è±«ã€‚å‡è®¾è¿™ä¸¤ç§å¼›è±«è§„å¾‹ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œè¿™å°±æ˜¯Onsagerçš„æ¶¨è½å›å½’å‡è®¾ã€‚æ¢è¨€ä¹‹ï¼Œå¯¹äºä¸€ä¸ªè¿‘å¹³è¡¡ä½“ç³»ï¼Œæ— æ³•åŒºåˆ†æ˜¯è‡ªå‘æ¶¨è½è¿˜æ˜¯åç¦»å¹³è¡¡åçš„å¼›è±«ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆè‡ªå‘æ¶¨è½è‡ªç›¸å…³çš„è¡Œä¸ºå®é™…ä¸Šåº”è¯¥ä¸tç¬é—´éå¹³è¡¡å‡å€¼åç¦»å¹³è¡¡çš„é‡è¡°å‡åˆ°å¹³è¡¡çš„è¡Œä¸ºæ˜¯ç›¸åŒçš„ã€‚

éå¹³è¡¡åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°Ï•(rN,â€†pN)

å¹³è¡¡æ€åˆ†å¸ƒfä¸éå¹³è¡¡æ€åˆ†å¸ƒÏ•åœ¨è¿‘å¹³è¡¡çš„èŒƒå›´å†…åº”å½“æœ‰ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\phi\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right)}{f\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right)}=\frac{A\left(t=0 ; \boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right)}{\langle A\rangle} \end{equation}$$ å³ï¼š $$\begin{align} \phi\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right)=\frac{A\left(t=0 ; \boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right)}{\langle A\rangle}f\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) \end{align}$$ å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \bar{A}(t) & =\int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r}^N \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{p}^N \phi\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) A\left(t ; \boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) \\ & =\langle A\rangle^{-1} \int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r}^N \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{p}^N f\left(\boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) A\left(0 ; \boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) A\left(t ; \boldsymbol{r}^N, \boldsymbol{p}^N\right) \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ å³ï¼š $$\begin{aligned} \bar{A}(t) =\langle A\rangle^{-1}\langle A(0)A(t)\rangle \end{aligned}$$

å¾—åˆ°ç¬æ—¶éå¹³è¡¡å‡å€¼åç¦»å¹³è¡¡çš„é‡ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \Delta \bar{A}(t) &\equiv \bar{A}(t)-\langle A\rangle=\langle A\rangle^{-1}\langle A(0) A(t)\rangle-\langle A\rangle \\ &=\langle A\rangle^{-1}\left\{\langle A(0) A(t)\rangle-\langle A\rangle^2\right\} \\ &=\langle A\rangle^{-1}\langle \delta A(0) \delta A(t)\rangle \\ &= \langle A\rangle^{-1}C(t) \\ C(t) &= \Delta \bar{A}(t)\langle A\rangle \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$

å°†è¯¥å­¤ç«‹ç³»ç»Ÿçš„åˆ†ææ‹“å±•åˆ°ä¸ç¯å¢ƒæœ‰æ¥è§¦çš„éå­¤ç«‹ç³»ç»Ÿã€‚æŠŠç³»ç»Ÿä¸ç¯å¢ƒçœ‹æˆæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ‹“å±•ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå°†æ‹“å±•ä½“ç³»è§†ä¸ºä¸€ä¸ªå­¤ç«‹çš„ä¸ªä½“ï¼š Eexâ€„=â€„Eâ€…+â€…Eb,â€†Vexâ€„=â€„Vâ€…+â€…Vb å…¶ä¸­ä¸‹æ ‡â€exâ€æŒ‡æ‹“å±•ä½“ç³»ï¼Œâ€œbâ€æŒ‡ç¯å¢ƒï¼Œæ— ä¸‹æ ‡æŒ‡ä½“ç³»ã€‚æ˜¾ç„¶å­˜åœ¨ä»¥ä¸‹å…³ç³»ï¼š Î”Eâ€„=â€„âˆ’Î”Eb,â€†Î”Vâ€„=â€„âˆ’Î”Vb,â€†Î”Nâ€„=â€„âˆ’Î”Nb ç”±äºæ‹“å±•ä½“ç³»æ˜¯å­¤ç«‹ä½“ç³»ï¼Œå› æ­¤ç†µåå·®å€¼ä¸ºï¼š Î”Sexâ€„=â€„Î”Sâ€…+â€…Î”Sb æœ‰ï¼š W(Î”Sex)â€„=â€„Wmaxe(Î”Sâ€…+â€…Î”Sb)/kB å‡è®¾ç¯å¢ƒè¶³å¤Ÿå¤§ï¼Œæœ‰ç¡®å®šçš„æ¸©åº¦Tå’Œå‹å¼ºpï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰ï¼š $$\begin{align} \Delta S_{\mathrm{b}}&=\frac{1}{T}\left(\Delta E_{\mathrm{b}}+p \Delta V_{\mathrm{b}}\right)=-\frac{1}{T}(\Delta E+p \Delta V) \\ W\left(\Delta S_{\mathrm{ex}}\right) &\equiv W(\Delta S, \Delta E, \Delta V)=W_{\max } \mathrm{e}^{\left(\Delta S+\Delta S_b\right) / k_{\mathrm{B}}}=W_{\max } \mathrm{e}^{(T \Delta S-\Delta E-p \Delta V) /\left(k_{\mathrm{B}} T\right)}\\ W &= W_{\max } \mathrm{e}^{-(\Delta F+p \Delta V) /\left(k_{\mathrm{B}} T\right)} \end{align}$$ è¿™æ˜¯å°é—­ä½“ç³»çš„Smoluchowskiå…¬å¼ã€‚

Boltzmannæ–¹ç¨‹

è®¨è®ºå•ç²’å­åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°éœ€è¦éµå®ˆçš„æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œå³Boltzmannæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œè¿™æ˜¯ç¨€è–„æ°”ä½“ä¸¥æ ¼çš„åŠ¨ç†è®ºçš„åŸºæœ¬æ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚ç”±è¯¥æ–¹ç¨‹å‡ºå‘ï¼Œä»åˆ†å­è´¨é‡ã€åˆ†å­é—´ç›¸äº’ä½œç”¨ï¼Œå¯å¾—åˆ°æŒ‡å®šæ¸©åº¦ä¸‹çš„æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°ã€å¯¼çƒ­ç³»æ•°ã€é»æ»ç³»æ•°ç­‰è¾“è¿æ€§è´¨ã€‚

  2. ç¢°æ’åˆ†æ ä»»æ„æ—¶åˆ»ã€ä»»æ„ä½ç½®ç¢°æ’å‰åç¬¬jç§ç»„åˆ†ç²’å­æ•°ä¸€å®šå®ˆæ’ï¼Œæ•…æœ‰ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} & f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}+\boldsymbol{v}_j \mathrm{~d} t, \boldsymbol{v}_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \mathrm{~d} t, t+\mathrm{d} t\right) \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \\ = & f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_j, t\right) \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j+\sum_i\left(\Gamma_{j i}^{(+)}-\Gamma_{j i}^{(-)}\right) \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \mathrm{~d} t \\ \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ å…¶ä¸­Î“ji(+)drdvjÂ dt,â€†Î“ji(âˆ’)drdvjÂ dtåˆ†åˆ«ä»£è¡¨æµå…¥çš„ä¸æµå‡ºç›¸ç©ºé—´çš„ç²’å­æ•°ã€‚ $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}+\boldsymbol{v}_j \mathrm{~d} t, \boldsymbol{v}_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \mathrm{~d} t, t+\mathrm{d} t\right)=&f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_j, t\right)+\frac{\partial f_j}{\partial t} \mathrm{~d} t+\nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f_j \cdot \boldsymbol{v}_j \mathrm{~d} t+\nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} f_j \cdot \frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \mathrm{~d} t \\ \frac{\partial f_j}{\partial t}+\boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} f_j=&\sum_i\left(\Gamma_{j i}^{(+)}-\Gamma_{j i}^{(-)}\right), \quad \forall j \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ ä¸Šé¢ä¾¿æ˜¯Boltzmannæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œä»£è¡¨ç¬¬jç§ç»„åˆ†ç²’å­Î¼ç©ºé—´çš„æ•°å¯†åº¦æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–è§„å¾‹ã€‚å·¦è¾¹æ˜¯éç¢°æ’æµåŠ¨å¯¹æ•°å¯†åº¦çš„è´¡çŒ®ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºæ¼‚ç§»é¡¹ï¼›å³è¾¹ä»£è¡¨ç¢°æ’å¯¹æ•°å¯†åº¦å˜åŒ–çš„è´¡çŒ®ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºç¢°æ’é¡¹ã€‚

    å½“ä½“ç³»å¤„äºå®šæ€çš„æ—¶å€™$\frac{\partial f_j}{\partial t}=0$ï¼Œæ•…Boltzmannæ–¹ç¨‹ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} f_j=\sum\left(\Gamma_{j i}^{(+)}-\Gamma_{j i}^{(-)}\right), \quad \forall j . \end{equation}$$

  3. ç¢°æ’é¡¹åˆ†æ å…·ä½“åˆ†æÎ“ji(+),â€†Î“ji(âˆ’)çš„è®¡ç®—æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œé’ˆå¯¹ç»„åˆ†jè®¡ç®—å…¶ç¢°æ’iç»„åˆ†ä¹‹åè„±ç¦»jç»„åˆ†ï¼Œè®°ä¸ºÎ“ji(âˆ’): Î“ji(âˆ’)â€„=â€„2Ï€âˆ¬fj(r,â€†vj,â€†t)fi(r,â€†vi,â€†t)|viâ€…âˆ’â€…vj|bÂ dbÂ dvi è¿™ä¸ªè¡¨è¾¾å¼å‡å®šäº†ç²’å­é€Ÿåº¦ä¸ä½ç½®æ— å…³ï¼Œç§°ä¸ºåˆ†å­æ··æ²Œå‡è®¾ã€‚è¿™æ˜¯è¯æ˜è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­è–„å¼±çš„åœ°æ–¹ã€‚ åŒç†ï¼Œè€ƒè™‘ç”±iç»„åˆ†ç¢°æ’æˆjç»„åˆ†çš„è´¡çŒ®ã€‚æœ€åå¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial f_j}{\partial t}+\boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} f_j=2 \pi \sum_i \int_b \int_{\boldsymbol{v}_i} b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_i\left|\boldsymbol{v}_i-\boldsymbol{v}_j\right|\left\{f_j^{\prime} f_i^{\prime}-f_j f_i\right\}, \quad \forall j \end{equation}$$ å…¶ä¸­ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \left\{\begin{aligned} f_i^{\prime} & \equiv f_i\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_i^{\prime}\left(\boldsymbol{v}_i, \boldsymbol{v}_j\right), t\right) \\ f_j^{\prime} & \equiv f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_j^{\prime}\left(\boldsymbol{v}_i, \boldsymbol{v}_j\right), t\right) \\ f_i & \equiv f_i\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_i, t\right) \\ f_j & \equiv f_j\left(\boldsymbol{r}, \boldsymbol{v}_j, t\right) \end{aligned}\right. \end{equation}$$

Enskogæ–¹ç¨‹

æ¥ä¸‹æ¥ä»Boltamannè¾“è¿æ–¹ç¨‹å‡ºå‘ï¼Œæ±‚æ··åˆç¨€è–„æ°”ä½“ä¸­çš„å„ç§è¾“è¿è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­ç²’å­Ïˆçš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–ï¼Œè¿™ä¾¿æ˜¯Enskogæ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚

æ€§è´¨çš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–

è€ƒè™‘jç»„åˆ†ç²’å­çš„æ€§è´¨Ïˆï¼Œå°†Boltzmannæ–¹ç¨‹ä¸¤è¾¹ä½œç”¨âˆ«dvjÏˆj(â‹…)å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} & \int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \psi_j\left[\frac{\partial f_j}{\partial t}+\boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_r f_j+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} f_j\right] \\ = & 2 \pi \sum_i \iiint \psi_j\left(f_j^{\prime} f_i^{\prime}-f_j f_i\right)\left|\boldsymbol{v}_i-\boldsymbol{v}_j\right| b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_i \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_j, \quad \forall j \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ å·¦è¾¹ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial}{\partial t} \int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \psi_j f_j-\int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j\left(\frac{\partial \psi_j}{\partial t}\right) $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \psi_j \boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f_j & =\nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} \cdot \int \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_j \psi_j ç»“åˆGausså®šå¾‹ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \iiint_V \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v} \nabla\left(\begin{array}{c} f \\ \cdot \boldsymbol{A} \\ \times \boldsymbol{A} \end{array}\right)=\oint_S \mathrm{~d} ç»“åˆä»¥ä¸Šä¸‰é¡¹å¾—åˆ°å…³äºjç»„åˆ†çš„Enskogæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} & \frac{\partial}{\partial t}\left(\rho_j\left\langle\psi_j\right\rangle\right)+\nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} \cdot\left(\rho_j\left\langle\psi_j \boldsymbol{v}_j\right\rangle\right)-\rho_j\left[\left\langle\frac{\partial \psi_j}{\partial t}\right\rangle+\left\langle\boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} \psi_j\right\rangle+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot\left\langle\nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} \psi_j\right\rangle\right] \\ = & 2 \pi \sum_i \iiint \psi_j\left(f_j^{\prime} f_i^{\prime}-f_j f_i\right)\left|\boldsymbol{v}_{\boldsymbol{i}}-\boldsymbol{v}_j\right| b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_i \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_j, \quad \forall j \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$

ä¸å˜é‡æ€§è´¨Ïˆçš„Enskogæ–¹ç¨‹

éƒ¨åˆ†æ€§è´¨åœ¨ç¢°æ’å‰åä¸å˜ï¼Œå³æ»¡è¶³ï¼š Ïˆi(vi)â€…+â€…Ïˆj(vj)â€„=â€„Ïˆiâ€²(viâ€²)â€…+â€…Ïˆjâ€²(vjâ€²),â€Šâ€âˆ€i,â€†j å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ä¸å˜é‡çš„å®šç†ï¼š âˆ‘i,â€†iâˆ­Ïˆj(fiâ€²fjâ€²â€…âˆ’â€…fifj)|viâ€…âˆ’â€…vj|bÂ dbÂ dviÂ dvjâ€„=â€„0 å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ä¸å˜é‡Ïˆçš„æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial}{\partial t} \sum_j \rho_j\left\langle\psi_j\right\rangle+\nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} \cdot \sum_j \rho_j\left\langle\psi_j \boldsymbol{v}_j\right\rangle-\sum_j \rho_j\left[\left\langle\frac{\partial \psi_j}{\partial t}\right\rangle+\left\langle\boldsymbol{v}_j \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} \psi_j\right\rangle+\frac{\boldsymbol{X}_j}{m_j} \cdot\left\langle\nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}_j} \psi_j\right\rangle\right]=0 \end{equation}$$

Boltzmannçš„Hå®šç†

è€ƒè™‘å•ç»„åˆ†ä½“ç³»ã€‚Boltxmannå®šä¹‰Hå‡½æ•°ä¸ºï¼š H(t)â€„â‰¡â€„âˆ¬drdvf(r,â€†v,â€†t)lnâ€†f(r,â€†v,â€†t) Hå‡½æ•°æœ¬è´¨ä¸Šå°±æ˜¯â€œè´Ÿç†µâ€ï¼Œä»¥ä¸‹ä»æœ¬ç« ç¬¬ä¸€èŠ‚çš„Boltamannç§¯åˆ†å¾®åˆ†æ–¹ç¨‹å‡ºå‘ï¼Œåˆ†æHå®šç†çš„ç‰©ç†å«ä¹‰ã€‚ Hå‡½æ•°å¯¹æ—¶é—´æ±‚å¯¼ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \frac{\mathrm{d} H}{\mathrm{~d} t}=&\iint \mathrm{d} r \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}\left(\frac{\partial f}{\partial t}\right)(1+\ln f) \\ =& -\iint \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}(1+\ln f) \boldsymbol{v} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{r}} f-\iint \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}(1+\ln f) \frac{\boldsymbol{X}}{m} \cdot \nabla_{\boldsymbol{v}} f \\ & +2 \pi \iiint \int \mathrm{d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v} b(1+\ln f)\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}-f f_1\right) \\ =& 2 \pi \iiint \int \mathrm{d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v} b(1+\ln f)\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}-f f_1\right) \\ =& 2 \pi \iiint \int \mathrm{d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v} b(1+\ln f)\left|\boldsymbol{v}-\boldsymbol{v}_1\right|\left(f_1^{\prime} f^{\prime}-f_1 f\right) \\ =&\frac{1}{2}[(\cdot)+(\cdot \cdot)] \\ =&2 \pi \iiint b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right| \frac{1}{2}\left(\left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}-f f_1\right)(1+\ln f)+\left(f_1^{\prime} f^{\prime}-f_1 f\right)\left(1+\ln f_1\right)\right) \\ =&\pi \iiint b \mathrm{d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}-f f_1\right)\left(2+\ln \left(f f_1\right)\right) \\ =&\pi \iiint \int b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} v_1 \mathrm{~d} r \mathrm{~d} v\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f\left(\boldsymbol{v}^{\prime}\right) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1^{\prime}\right)-f(\boldsymbol{v}) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1\right)\right)\left[2+\ln \left(f(\boldsymbol{v}) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1\right)\right)\right] \\ =&\pi \iiint \int b^{\prime} \mathrm{d} b^{\prime} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}_1^{\prime} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}^{\prime}\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1^{\prime}-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f(\boldsymbol{v}) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1\right)-f\left(\boldsymbol{v}^{\prime}\right) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1^{\prime}\right)\right)\left[2+\ln \left(f\left(\boldsymbol{v}^{\prime}\right) f\left(\boldsymbol{v}_1^{\prime}\right)\right)\right] \\ =& \pi \iiint \int b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|\left(f f_1-f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}\right)\left(2+\ln \left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}\right)\right) \\ =& \pi \iiint \int b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} r \mathrm{~d} v\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right| \frac{1}{2}\left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}-f f_1\right)\left[\ln \left(f f_1\right)-\ln \left(f^{\prime} f_1^{\prime}\right)\right] \\ =& \frac{\pi}{2} \iiint \int b \mathrm{~d} b \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{v}_1 \mathrm{~d} \boldsymbol{r} \mathrm{d} \boldsymbol{v}\left|\boldsymbol{v}_1-\boldsymbol{v}\right|(x-y) \ln \left(\frac{y}{x}\right) \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$

å•ä½æ—¶é—´å†…ä½“ç³»y1è½¬ç§»åˆ°y2çš„æ¡ä»¶æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ï¼Œæ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦è·ƒè¿é€Ÿåº¦Wt(y1,â€†y2)ï¼š $$\begin{equation} W_t\left(y_1, y_2\right) \equiv \lim _{\tau \rightarrow 0}\left\{\frac{P_{1 \mid 1}\left(y_2, t_1+\tau \mid y_1, t_1\right)}{\tau}\right\}_{y_1 \neq y_2} \end{equation}$$

Pauliä¸»æ–¹ç¨‹ï¼ˆMaster equationï¼‰ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial P_1\left(y_2, t\right)}{\partial t}=\int_{\text {all } y_1} \mathrm{~d} y_1\left\{W_t\left(y_1, y_2\right) P_1\left(y_1, t\right)-W_t\left(y_2, y_1\right) P_1\left(y_2, t\right)\right\} \end{equation}$$ å³è¾¹ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹è¡¨ç¤ºä»å…¶å®ƒæ€åˆ°y2ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒé¡¹è¡¨ç¤ºä»y2å˜åŒ–åˆ°å…¶å®ƒæ€çš„é¡¹ã€‚ä¸»æ–¹ç¨‹å°±æ˜¯Markovè¿‡ç¨‹æ¦‚ç‡åˆ†å¸ƒçš„æ—¶é—´æ¼”åŒ–ã€‚

Fokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹

ç•¥å»è·ƒè¿é€Ÿåº¦çš„ä¸‹æ ‡ï¼Œè®¤ä¸ºè·ƒè¿é€Ÿåº¦å–å†³äºåˆæ€åŠå…¶è·ƒè¿å¹…åº¦Î¾â€„â‰¡â€„yâ€…âˆ’â€…yâ€²ã€‚ W(yâ€²,â€†y)â€„â‰¡â€„W(yâ€²;â€†yâ€…âˆ’â€…yâ€²)â€„=â€„W(yâ€²;â€†Î¾)

åˆ©ç”¨å˜åŒ–ä¸Taylorå±•å¼€ï¼Œå¯å°†ä¸»æ–¹ç¨‹æ”¹å†™ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \frac{\partial P_1(y, t)}{\partial t}= & \int \mathrm{d} \xi P_1(y, t) W(y ; \xi)+\sum_{n=1}^{\infty} \frac{(-1)^n}{n !} \frac{\partial^n}{\partial y^n}\left[P_1(y, t) \int \mathrm{d} \xi \xi^n W(y ; \xi)\right] \\ & -P_1(y, t) \int \mathrm{d} \xi W(y ;-\xi) \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$

å¯ä»¥å‡å®šï¼Œå½“|Î¾|å˜å¤§æ—¶ï¼Œè·ƒè¿é€Ÿåº¦Wä¼šå¾ˆå¿«å˜å°ã€‚

P1(yâ€…+â€…Î”y,â€†t)â€„â‰ƒâ€„P1(y,â€†t),â€Šâ€âˆ€|Î”y|â€„<â€„Î´, å¾—åˆ°W(y;â€†Î¾)â€„=â€„W(y;â€†âˆ’Î¾)ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶ä»¤ Î±n(y)â€„â‰¡â€„âˆ«dÎ¾Î¾nW(y;â€†Î¾)

å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial P_1(y, t)}{\partial t}=\sum_{n=1}^{\infty} \frac{(-1)^n}{n !} \frac{\partial^n}{\partial y^n}\left[\alpha_n(y) P_1(y, t)\right] \end{equation}$$

å¦‚æœåªå–åˆ°äºŒæ¬¡ç»Ÿè®¡çŸ©ï¼Œå¿½ç•¥é«˜é˜¶ç»Ÿè®¡çŸ©ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°ä½†å˜çš„Fokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial P_1(y, t)}{\partial t} \simeq-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left[\alpha_1(y) P_1(y, t)\right]+\frac{1}{2} \frac{\partial^2}{\partial y^2}\left[\alpha_2(y) P_1(y, t)\right] \end{equation}$$

å½“æœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå˜é‡æ—¶ï¼Œå¯¹åº”Chapman-Kolmogorovæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼š P1â€…âˆ£â€…1(x3,â€†y3,â€†t3â€…âˆ£â€…x1,â€†y1,â€†t1)â€„=â€„âˆ«dx2Â dy2P1â€…âˆ£â€…1(x3,â€†y3,â€†t3â€…âˆ£â€…x2,â€†y2,â€†t2)P1â€…âˆ£â€…1(x2,â€†y2,â€†t2â€…âˆ£â€…x1,â€†y1,â€†t1)

åŒç†, å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°å¯¹åº”çš„ Fokker-Planck æ–¹ç¨‹ $$ \begin{aligned} \frac{\partial P_1(x, y, t)}{\partial t}= & -\frac{\partial}{\partial x}\left[\alpha_1 P_1(x, y, t)\right]-\frac{\partial}{\partial y}\left[\beta_1 P_1(x, y, t)\right] \\ & +\frac{1}{2} \frac{\partial^2}{\partial x^2}\left[\alpha_2 P_1(x, y, t)\right]+\frac{1}{2} \frac{\partial^2}{\partial y^2}\left[\beta_2 P_1(x, y, t)\right]+\frac{\partial^2}{\partial x \partial y}\left[\gamma P_1(x, y, t)\right] \end{aligned} $$

å…¶ä¸­ $$ \begin{aligned} \alpha_n(x, y) & \equiv \iint \mathrm{d} \xi \mathrm{d} \zeta \xi^n W(x, y ; \xi, \zeta) \\ \beta_n(x, y) & \equiv \iint \mathrm{d} \xi \mathrm{d} \zeta \zeta^n W(x, y ; \xi, \zeta) \\ \gamma(x, y) & \equiv \iint \mathrm{d} \xi \mathrm{d} \zeta \xi \zeta W(x, y ; \xi, \zeta) \end{aligned} $$

Brownè¿åŠ¨ç†è®ºçš„åŸºæœ¬æ–¹ç¨‹ç§°ä¸ºLangevinæ–¹ç¨‹ï¼Œå«æœ‰éšæœºåŠ›ä¸æ‘©æ“¦åŠ›ã€‚æ¶¨è½è€—æ•£å®šç†æŠŠè¿™äº›åŠ›è”ç³»èµ·æ¥ã€‚è¿™æ ·ä¸€ç±»å¼•å…¥éšæœºè¿‡ç¨‹ç”¨æ¥å¤„ç†å¤æ‚ä½“ç³»ï¼Œæˆ–å¯¹åŒä¸€ä½“ç³»ç›¸å®è§‚æ–¹å‘æé«˜æè¿°çš„å±‚æ¬¡ï¼Œä»è€Œè¾¾åˆ°ç²—ç²’åŒ–ç›®çš„çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå°±æ˜¯æ¨å¹¿æ„ä¹‰ä¸Šçš„Brownè¿åŠ¨ã€‚

æ— å¤–åœºLangevinæ–¹ç¨‹

$$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} &m \dot{\boldsymbol{v}}=-m \zeta \boldsymbol{v}+\boldsymbol{f}(t)\\ &\dot{\boldsymbol{v}}=-\zeta \boldsymbol{v}+\frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t)}{m} \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ å…¶ä¸­f(t)æ˜¯éšæœºåŠ›ï¼Œâˆ’mÎ¶væ˜¯ç²˜æ»åŠ›ï¼ˆæ‘©æ“¦åŠ›ï¼‰ï¼Œè¯¥æ–¹ç¨‹ç§°ä¸ºæ— å¤–åœºLangevinæ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚

åˆ©ç”¨Laplaceå˜æ¢ï¼š $$ \begin{gathered} s \tilde{\boldsymbol{v}}(s)-\boldsymbol{v}(0)=-\zeta \tilde{\boldsymbol{v}}(s)+\mathcal{L}\left(\frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t)}{m}\right) \\ \tilde{\boldsymbol{v}}(s)=(s+\zeta)^{-1} \tilde{\boldsymbol{v}}(0)+(s+\zeta)^{-1} \mathcal{L}\left(\frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t)}{m}\right) \end{gathered} $$

å†åˆ©ç”¨åå˜æ¢å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$ \boldsymbol{v}(t)=\mathrm{e}^{-\zeta t} \boldsymbol{v}(0)+\mathrm{e}^{-\zeta t} * \mathcal{L}\left(\frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t)}{m}\right) $$ $$ \boldsymbol{v}(t)=\mathrm{e}^{-\zeta t} \boldsymbol{v}(0)+\int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta(t-\tau)} \frac{\boldsymbol{f}(\tau)}{m} $$ å³è¾¹ç¬¬ä¸€é¡¹ç»™å‡ºäº†åˆå§‹é€Ÿåº¦çš„è¡°å‡ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒé¡¹ç»™å‡ºäº†éšæœºåŠ›é€ æˆçš„é€Ÿåº¦ã€‚

å‡è®¾éšæœºåŠ›çš„å¹³å‡å€¼å’Œå®ƒçš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°æœä»ä»¥ä¸‹å…³ç³»ï¼š âŸ¨f(t)âŸ©â€„=â€„0 and âŸ¨f(t)â€…â‹…â€…f(tâ€²)âŸ©â€„=â€„Ï•(tâ€…âˆ’â€…tâ€²),

é€Ÿåº¦çš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°

æ¥ä¸‹æ¥è€ƒè™‘Brownè¿åŠ¨ä½“ç³»å¤„äºç¨³æ€æ—¶é•¿æ—¶é—´çš„é€Ÿåº¦çš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ã€‚

å½“tâ€„â†’â€„âˆæ—¶ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒé¡¹è¿›è¡Œå˜é‡æ›¿æ¢uâ€„â‰¡â€„tâ€…âˆ’â€…Ï„ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \lim _{t \rightarrow \infty} \boldsymbol{v}(t) &\simeq \lim _{t \rightarrow \infty} \int_t^0(-\mathrm{d} u) \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta u} \frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t-u)}{m}\\ &=\frac{1}{m} \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta u} f(t-u) \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ é€Ÿåº¦çš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç”¨æ—¶é—´å¹³å‡å¯è¡¨ç¤ºä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle &= \lim _{\tau \rightarrow \infty} \frac{1}{\tau} \int_0^\tau \mathrm{d} s \boldsymbol{v}(t+s) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}+s\right) \\ &=\lim _{\tau \rightarrow \infty} \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_1 \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_2 \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left(u_1+u_2\right)} \frac{1}{\tau} \int_0^\tau \mathrm{d} s \frac{1}{m^2} \boldsymbol{f}\left(t+s-u_1\right) \cdot \boldsymbol{f}\left(t^{\prime}+s-u_2\right) \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$ è€ƒè™‘éšæœºåŠ›çš„æ€§è´¨ï¼š âŸ¨f(t)â€…â‹…â€…f(tâ€²)âŸ©â€„=â€„Ï•(tâ€…âˆ’â€…tâ€²)â€„â‰ƒâ€„Î»Î´(tâ€…âˆ’â€…tâ€²)

è¿›ä¸€æ­¥å¾—åˆ° $$ \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle=\int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_1 \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_2 \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left(u_1+u_2\right)} \lim _{\tau \rightarrow \infty} \frac{1}{\tau} \int_0^\tau \mathrm{d} s \frac{1}{m^2} \lambda \delta\left[\left(t-u_1\right)-\left(t^{\prime}-u_2\right)\right], $$

å…¶ä¸­å¯¹ s çš„ç§¯åˆ†ä¸º $$ \begin{aligned} \lim _{\tau \rightarrow \infty} \frac{1}{\tau} \int_0^\tau \mathrm{d} s \frac{1}{m^2} \lambda \delta\left[\left(t-u_1\right)-\left(t^{\prime}-u_2\right)\right] & =\frac{\lambda}{m^2} \delta\left[\left(t-t^{\prime}\right)-\left(u_1-u_2\right)\right] \lim _{\tau \rightarrow \infty} \frac{1}{\tau} \int_0^\tau \mathrm{d} s \\ & =\frac{\lambda}{m^2} \delta\left[u_2-\left(u_1-t+t^{\prime}\right)\right], \end{aligned} $$

è¿›è€Œ $$ \begin{aligned} \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle & =\int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_1 \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_2 \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left(u_1+u_2\right)} \frac{\lambda}{m^2} \delta\left[u_2-\left(u_1-t+t^{\prime}\right)\right] \\ & =\frac{\lambda}{m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left(t^{\prime}-t\right)} \int_0^{\infty} \mathrm{d} u_1 \mathrm{e}^{-2 \zeta u_1} . \end{aligned} $$

æœ€å³è¾¹çš„ç§¯åˆ†ç­‰äº 1/(2Î¶), äºæ˜¯å¾—åˆ° $$ \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle=\frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left(t^{\prime}-t\right)} . $$

åˆå› ä¸ºå¿…æœ‰ âŸ¨v(t)â€…â‹…â€…v(tâ€²)âŸ©â€„=â€„âŸ¨v(tâ€²)â€…â‹…â€…v(t)âŸ©, æ•…å¾—åˆ° $$ \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle=\frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left|t^{\prime}-t\right|}, $$

å³æ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°å–å†³äºæ—¶é—´é—´éš”çš„ç»å¯¹å€¼ |tâ€…âˆ’â€…tâ€²|. ç°åœ¨, å†æ ¹æ® Brown è¿åŠ¨ä¸­çš„æ¶¨è½è€—æ•£å®šç†, å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ç¨³æ€æ—¶ Brown ç²’å­é€Ÿåº¦çš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ä¸º $$ \left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle=\frac{3 k_{\mathrm{B}} T}{m} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left|t^{\prime}-t\right|} . $$

æ ¹æ®Doobå®šç†ï¼Œè‹¥Gaussè¿‡ç¨‹çš„è‡ªç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°æ˜¯æŒ‡æ•°å½¢çš„ã€‚åˆ™è¯¥è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸€å®šæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªMarkovè¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚

Brownç²’å­çš„å‡æ–¹ä½ç§»

å¾—åˆ°äº†ç¨³æ€æ—¶ Brown ç²’å­é€Ÿåº¦çš„è‡ªæ—¶é—´ç›¸å…³å‡½æ•°ä¹‹å, å°±å¯ä»¥æ±‚è§£ Brown è¿åŠ¨ä¸­ç²’å­ä½ç§»å¹³æ–¹çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡å€¼, ç®€ç§°å‡æ–¹ä½ç§»(MSD). å› ä¸ºé€Ÿåº¦æ˜¯ä½ç½®çš„ä¸€é˜¶å¯¼æ•°, å³ $$ \left\langle\dot{\boldsymbol{r}}(t) \cdot \dot{\boldsymbol{r}}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle=\left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle \quad \text { å’Œ } \quad \boldsymbol{r}(t)=\int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau \boldsymbol{v}(\tau), $$

äºæ˜¯æ±‚è§£ç¨³æ€ (å³ tâ€„â‰«â€„Î¶âˆ’1 ) æ—¶ Brown ç²’å­çš„å‡æ–¹ä½ç§» âŸ¨r(t)2âŸ©, åªéœ€å¯¹é€Ÿåº¦è‡ªç›¸å…³ç§¯åˆ†ä¸¤æ¬¡, å³ $$ \begin{aligned} \left\langle r(t)^2\right\rangle=\lim _{t \rightarrow t^{\prime}}\left\langle\boldsymbol{r}(t) \cdot \boldsymbol{r}\left(t^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle & =\lim _{t \rightarrow t^{\prime}} \int_0^{t^{\prime}} \mathrm{d} \tau^{\prime} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau\left\langle\boldsymbol{v}(\tau) \cdot \boldsymbol{v}\left(\tau^{\prime}\right)\right\rangle \\ & =\lim _{t \rightarrow t^{\prime}} \int_0^{t^{\prime}} \mathrm{d} \tau^{\prime} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau \frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left|\tau-\tau^{\prime}\right|}, \end{aligned} $$

å³ $$ \left\langle r(t)^2\right\rangle=\int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau^{\prime} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau \frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta \mid \tau-\tau^{\prime}} . $$

å¼ (13.1.3-1) ä¸­çš„ç§¯åˆ†å±äº Iâ€„=â€„âˆ«0tÂ dÏ„âˆ«0tÂ dÏ„â€²f(Ï„â€…âˆ’â€…Ï„â€²) ç±»å‹, å¯ä»¥è¯æ˜, æ­¤ç±»ç§¯åˆ†æœ‰å¦‚ä¸‹æ€§è´¨: âˆ«0tÂ dÏ„âˆ«0tÂ dÏ„â€²f(Ï„â€…âˆ’â€…Ï„â€²)â€„=â€„âˆ«0tÂ du(tâ€…âˆ’â€…u)[f(u)â€…+â€…f(âˆ’u)]

å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$ \begin{aligned} \left\langle r(t)^2\right\rangle & =\int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau^{\prime} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} \tau \frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta\left|\tau-\tau^{\prime}\right|}=\int_0^t \mathrm{~d} u(t-u)\left[\frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta|u|}+\frac{\lambda}{2 \zeta m^2} \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta|-u|}\right] \\ & =\frac{\lambda}{\zeta m^2} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} u(t-u) \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta|u|}=\frac{\lambda}{\zeta m^2} \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} u(t-u) \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta u} . \end{aligned} $$

å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥ç§¯åˆ†å¾—åˆ°å…¶ä¸­çš„ $$ \int_0^t \mathrm{~d} u(t-u) \mathrm{e}^{-\zeta u}=\frac{t}{\zeta}+\frac{1}{\zeta^2}\left(\mathrm{e}^{-\zeta t}-1\right) . $$

äºæ˜¯ $$ \left\langle r(t)^2\right\rangle=\frac{\lambda}{\zeta m^2}\left[\frac{t}{\zeta}+\frac{1}{\zeta^2}\left(\mathrm{e}^{-\zeta t}-1\right)\right] . $$

åœ¨æ—¶é—´è¾ƒé•¿çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹æœ‰ $$ \lim _{t \rightarrow \infty}\left\langle r^2(t)\right\rangle \simeq \frac{\lambda}{\zeta^2 m^2} t . $$

è‡³æ­¤, ç†è®ºæŠŠ Langevin æ–¹ç¨‹ä¸­çš„æ‘©æ“¦ç³»æ•° Î¶m, éšæœºåŠ›å¼ºåº¦ Î» ä¸å‡æ–¹ä½ç§»è”ç³»èµ·æ¥äº†, è¿˜æ²¡æœ‰è”ç³»åˆ°æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•° D.

å”¯è±¡è§„å¾‹ä¸­çš„æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°

æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°Dçš„æ¦‚å¿µæ˜¯ä»å®éªŒä¸­å¼•å…¥ã€‚ Ïvâ€„=â€„âˆ’Dâˆ‡Ï å…¶ä¸­Ï(r,â€†t)è¡¨ç¤ºtæ—¶åˆ»rå¤„å•ä½æº¶æ¶²ä½“ç§¯å†…æº¶è´¨çš„ç²’å­æ•°ï¼Œå³æ•°å¯†åº¦ï¼›vä¸ºæº¶è´¨ç²’å­çš„é€Ÿåº¦ï¼›Dä¸ºæ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°ï¼Œå‡†ç¡®ç‚¹ä¸ºå¹³åŠ¨æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°ã€‚ä¸Šå¼ç§°ä¸ºFickç¬¬ä¸€å®šå¾‹ã€‚

å¦ä¸€æ–¹é¢ï¼Œä»ç²’å­æ•°å®ˆæ’æ–¹ç¨‹å‡ºå‘ï¼š $$\begin{align} 0=&\frac{\partial \rho}{\partial t}+ \nabla\cdot(\rho \boldsymbol{v}) \\ =& \frac{\partial \rho}{\partial t}+ \nabla\cdot(-D\nabla\rho) \\ =& \frac{\partial \rho}{\partial t}-D \nabla\cdot\nabla\rho \\ \frac{\partial \rho}{\partial t}=&D \nabla^2\rho \end{align}$$ ç§°ä¸ºFickç¬¬äºŒå®šå¾‹ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºæº¶æ¶²ä¸­ä»»æ„ä¸€å¤„æº¶è´¨æ•°å¯†åº¦éšæ—¶é—´çš„å¢é€Ÿæ­£æ¯”äºâˆ‡2Ïï¼Œæ¯”ä¾‹ç³»æ•°ä¸ºå¹³åŠ¨æ‰©æ•£ç³»æ•°ã€‚

ä»¥ä¸‹å‡è®¾åˆå§‹æƒ…å†µï¼ˆtâ€„=â€„0ï¼‰Nä¸ªç²’å­å†r0å¤„ï¼š Ï(r,â€†0)â€„=â€„NÎ´(râ€…âˆ’â€…r0) å†è®¾G(r,â€†t)drä¸ºtæ—¶åˆ»åœ¨å¾®ä½“ç§¯drä¸­å‡ºç°æº¶è´¨ç²’å­çš„æ¦‚ç‡ï¼Œäºæ˜¯ï¼š $$\begin{equation} G(r, t) = \frac{\rho(r, t)}{N} \end{equation}$$ å› æ­¤ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{\partial G(r, t)}{\partial t}=&D \nabla^2G(r, t) \\ G(r, 0) =& \delta(r-r_0) \end{align}$$ åˆ©ç”¨å‚…é‡Œå¶å˜æ¢è§£å¾—ï¼š $$\begin{equation} G(r, t)=\left(\frac{1}{2 \pi}\right)^3\left(\frac{\pi}{D t}\right)^{3 / 2} \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{\left|r-r_0\right|^2}{4 D t}} \end{equation}$$

ä»»æ„ç‰©ç†é‡A(r)çš„ç³»ç»¼å¹³å‡ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle A\rangle = \int_\Omega dr A(r)G(r, t) \end{align}$$

ä»Langevinæ–¹ç¨‹åˆ°Fokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹

æ— å¤–åœºLangevinæ–¹ç¨‹çš„Fokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹

è®¾Brownç²’å­çš„é€Ÿåº¦å¹³å‡ä¸ºÎ¾ï¼Œåœ¨tæ—¶åˆ»ç²’å­é€Ÿåº¦å¤„äº|Î¾,â€†Î¾â€…+â€…dÎ¾|çš„æ¦‚ç‡ä¸ºP(Î¾,â€†t)ï¼Œæ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦çš„å®šä¹‰ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} P(\xi, t)\equiv \langle\delta(\xi-v(t))\rangle \end{align}$$ å¯†åº¦ä¸æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ä¹‹é—´çš„å¯¹åº”å…³ç³»ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} \begin{array}{ccccc} \hline \rho(\boldsymbol{r})=\sum_{i=1}^N \delta\left(\boldsymbol{r}-\boldsymbol{r}_{\boldsymbol{i}}\right) & \rho(\boldsymbol{r}) & \boldsymbol{r} & \boldsymbol{r}_i & \sum_{i=1}^N(\cdot) \\ \hline P(\boldsymbol{\xi}, t) \equiv\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))\rangle & P(\boldsymbol{\xi}, t) & \boldsymbol{\xi} & \boldsymbol{v}(t) & \langle\cdot\rangle \\ \hline \end{array} \end{equation}$$ æ±‚æŸç‰©ç†é‡çš„è¿åŠ¨æ–¹ç¨‹å°±æ˜¯æ±‚Pçš„æ—¶é—´åå¯¼æ•°ã€‚

$$\begin{equation} \begin{aligned} \frac{\partial}{\partial t} P(\boldsymbol{\xi}, t)&=-\frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t)) \dot{\boldsymbol{v}}(t)\rangle \\ & =\frac{\partial\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))\rangle}{\partial(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))} \frac{\partial(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))}{\partial t}=\frac{\partial\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))\rangle}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}[-\dot{\boldsymbol{v}}(t)] \\ & =-\frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t)) \dot{\boldsymbol{v}}(t)\rangle \\ & =-\frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\left\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))\left(-\zeta \boldsymbol{\xi}+\frac{\boldsymbol{f}(t)}{m}\right)\right\rangle \\ & =\frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\{\zeta \boldsymbol{\xi}\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t))\rangle\}-\frac{1}{m} \frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t)) \boldsymbol{f}(t)\rangle \\ & =\frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}[\zeta P(\boldsymbol{\xi}, t) \boldsymbol{\xi}]-\frac{1}{m} \frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{\xi}}\langle\delta(\boldsymbol{\xi}-\boldsymbol{v}(t)) \boldsymbol{f}(t)\rangle \end{aligned} \end{equation}$$

å‡è®¾éšæœºåŠ›çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ä¸ºGaussåˆ†å¸ƒï¼š $$\begin{equation} P[\boldsymbol{f}(t)]=\exp \left\{-\int_{t_0}^{t_f} \mathrm{~d} t \frac{f^2(t)}{4 \zeta m k_{\mathrm{B}} T}\right\} \end{equation}$$ å…¶ä¸­ t0,â€†tf åˆ†åˆ«ä¸º f(t) çš„åˆå§‹æ—¶é—´å’Œç»“æŸæ—¶é—´. ä¸ºäº†ç†è§£æ³›å‡½å‹çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦, è¦å¯¹ Gauss åˆ†å¸ƒå¤šä½œäº›è§£é‡Š: å› ä¸ºè¿™é‡Œæ•´ä¸ªèŒƒå›´å†…çš„éšæœºåŠ›å‡½æ•° f(t) éƒ½ä¸ä¸€ä¸ªæ ‡é‡ P å¯¹åº”, æ‰€ä»¥è¿™æ ·çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ³›å‡½ P[f(t)], è€Œä¸æ˜¯å¤åˆå‡½æ•° P(f(t)) ã€‚ ç›¸åº”åœ°, æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦çš„å½’ä¸€åŒ–æ˜¯æ³›å‡½ç§¯åˆ†ã€‚

  1. å¯¹äºä¸€ä¸ªéšæœºå˜é‡å½’ä¸€åŒ–çš„ Gauss åˆ†å¸ƒ N(Î¼,â€†Ïƒ2), å…¶æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ (å‡½æ•°) ä¸º $$ f(x)=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2 \pi \sigma^2}} \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{(z-\mu)^2}{2 \sigma^2}} $$ å®ƒæ»¡è¶³ âˆ«âˆ’âˆâˆdxf(x)â€„=â€„1ã€‚

  2. æ¨å¹¿åˆ° n ä¸ªéšæœºå˜é‡ x1,â€†x2,â€†â‹¯,â€†xn (ä»¤åˆ—é˜µ xâ€„â‰¡â€„[x1,â€†x2,â€†â‹¯,â€†xn]T ) å½’ä¸€åŒ–çš„ Gauss åˆ†å¸ƒ N(Î¼,â€†S), å…¶æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ (å‡½æ•°) ä¸º $$ f(\boldsymbol{x})=\frac{1}{(2 \pi|\boldsymbol{S}|)^{n / 2}} \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{1}{2}(\boldsymbol{x}-\boldsymbol{\mu})^{\mathrm{T}} S^{-1}(\boldsymbol{x}-\boldsymbol{\mu})} $$

    å…¶ä¸­ Î¼â€„â‰¡â€„[Î¼1,â€†Î¼2,â€†â‹¯,â€†Î¼n]T ä¸ºæ‰€æœ‰å¹³å‡å€¼æ’æˆçš„åˆ—é˜µ, åæ–¹å·®é˜µ $\boldsymbol{S} \equiv \frac{1}{n-1}(\boldsymbol{x}-$ Î¼)(xâ€…âˆ’â€…Î¼)Tã€‚

    åœ¨ç°åœ¨çš„æƒ…å†µ (è§å¼ (13.2.1-4)) ä¸‹, éšæœºå˜é‡ä¸æ˜¯ç¦»æ•£å‹çš„, è€Œæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªè¿ç»­å‹çš„å‡½æ•° f(t), ç›¸å½“äºæ— ç©·å¤šä¸ªäº’ä¸ºç‹¬ç«‹çš„éšæœºè‡ªå˜é‡. ä¸æ­¤å¯¹åº”, å¯¹äº n ä¸ªç‹¬ç«‹çš„éšæœºè‡ªå˜é‡, å¹¶ä¸”å‡å€¼ Î¼â€„=â€„0 å’Œ Sâ€„=â€„2Î“kBT1 çš„æƒ…å†µ, å¼ (13.2.1-6) åº”è¯¥æ¨å¹¿ã€æ”¹å†™ä¸º $$ f(\boldsymbol{x})=\frac{1}{\left(4 \pi \Gamma k_{\mathrm{B}} T\right)^{n / 2}} \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{1}{4 \Gamma k_{\mathrm{B}} T} \sum_{i=1}^n x_i^2} . $$

  3. å†ä»ç¦»æ•£å‹æ¨å¹¿åˆ°è¿ç»­å‹éšæœºå˜é‡ x(t) å°±å¾—åˆ°æ³›å‡½å‹çš„æ¦‚ç‡å¯†åº¦ä¸º $$ f[x(t)]=C \exp \left\{-\int_{t_0}^{t_f} \mathrm{~d} t \frac{x^2(t)}{4 \Gamma k_{\mathrm{B}} T}\right\}, $$

    å…¶ä¸­ C ä¸ºå½’ä¸€åŒ–å¸¸æ•°, t0,â€†tf åˆ†åˆ«ä¸º x(t) çš„åˆå§‹æ—¶é—´å’Œç»“æŸæ—¶é—´ã€‚

æ­¤å¤„çœç•¥å¾ˆå¤šåŒ–ç®€æ­¥éª¤

æœ€ç»ˆå¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{equation} \frac{\partial}{\partial t} P(\boldsymbol{v}, t)=\zeta \frac{\partial}{\partial \boldsymbol{v}}[P(\boldsymbol{v}, t) \boldsymbol{v}]+\zeta \frac{k_{\mathrm{B}} T}{m} \frac{\partial^2}{\partial v^2} P(\boldsymbol{v}, t) \end{equation}$$ ç§°ä¸ºFokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹ã€‚

è¿‡é˜»å°¼Langevinæ–¹ç¨‹çš„Smoluchowskiæ–¹ç¨‹

æœ‰å¤–åœºLangevinæ–¹ç¨‹çš„Fokker-Plankæ–¹ç¨‹

è‡ªç”±Brownè¿åŠ¨çš„Fokker-Planckæ–¹ç¨‹çš„ä¸¥æ ¼è§£

çº¿æ€§å“åº”ç†è®º

é™æ€å“åº”ï¼šå¤–åœºä¸éšæ—¶é—´å˜åŒ–ï¼Œåˆ™ä½“ç³»ä¼šåœ¨è¯¥æ’å®šå¤–åœºä¹‹ä¸‹è¾¾åˆ°æ–°çš„å¹³è¡¡æ€ï¼Œæ±‚è¿™æ ·å“åº”çš„å¹³è¡¡ç»Ÿè®¡åŠ›å­¦é—®é¢˜ã€‚

åŠ¨æ€å“åº”ï¼šæ±‚ä½“ç³»å¯¹å¤–åœºçš„ç¬æ—¶å“åº”ï¼Œæˆ–è€…å‘¨æœŸæ€§å¤–åœºã€‚

ä»¥ä¸‹å…ˆè®¨è®ºä½“ç³»å¯¹é™æ€å¤–åœºçš„å“åº”ï¼Œç„¶åè®¨è®ºå¯¹å«æ—¶å¤–åœºå“åº”çš„Green-Kuboçº¿æ€§å“åº”ç†è®ºã€‚

é™æ€çº¿æ€§å“åº”

è®¨è®ºå¦‚ä½•æ±‚å¹³è¡¡çš„çº¿æ€§å“åº”ã€‚

è®¾ä½“ç³»åœ¨æœªå—æ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶çš„ Hamilton é‡ä¸º H0(x),å…¶ä¸­ xâ€„â‰¡â€„{q,â€†p},â€†qâ€„â‰¡â€„{q1,â€†q2,â€†â‹¯,â€†q3N},â€†pâ€„â‰¡â€„{p2,â€†p2,â€†â‹¯,â€†p3N}, è®°æ’å®šå¤–åœºä¸º E. ä½“ç³»å—æ‰°åŠ¨åçš„èƒ½é‡å¢é‡, å³ä½“ç³»ä¸å¤–åœºè€¦åˆçš„èƒ½é‡, è®¾ä¸º Hâ€²â€„=â€„âˆ’A(x)E, å…¶ä¸­ A(x)ä¸ºä½“ç³»çŠ¶æ€çš„æŸä¸ªä¸ E å…±è½­çš„å·²çŸ¥å‡½æ•°. â€œå…±è½­â€ æ˜¯æŒ‡è‹¥ E æ˜¯å¤–ç”µåœºçš„ç”µåœºå¼ºåº¦ E, åˆ™ A å°±æ˜¯ä½“ç³»æ€»çš„ç”µå¶æçŸ© Î¼. ä¸å¤–ç£åœºå¼ºåº¦ H å…±è½­çš„æ˜¯ä½“ç³»çš„æ€»ç£çŸ© M.å¯¹åº”çš„æ‰°åŠ¨èƒ½é‡ä¸º Hâ€²â€„=â€„âˆ’Î¼â€…â‹…â€…E å’Œ Hâ€²â€„=â€„âˆ’Mâ€…â‹…â€…H. å®é™…ä¸Š, åœ¨ä»¥ä¸‹è®¨è®ºä¸­, E å’Œ Açš„å…·ä½“å½¢å¼å¹¶ä¸é‡è¦. æ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶ä½“ç³»çš„ Hamilton é‡ä¸º H(x,â€†E)â€„=â€„H0â€…+â€…Hâ€²â€„=â€„H0(x)â€…âˆ’â€…A(x)E

ç»å…¸åŠ›å­¦ä¸­çš„é™æ€çº¿æ€§å“åº”

è®¾æœªæ‰°åŠ¨çš„åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°f(x)ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} f(x) = \frac{1}{Q}\mathbb{e}^{-\beta H_0(x)} \end{align}$$ å…¶ä¸­Qâ€„=â€„âˆ«dxeâˆ’Î²H0(x)ä¸ºæœªæ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶ä½“ç³»çš„é…åˆ†å‡½æ•°ï¼Œxâ€„â‰¡â€„(q,â€†p)è¡¨ç¤ºÎ“ç›¸ç©ºé—´å˜é‡ã€‚æœªæ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶ï¼Œè‹¥ä½“ç³»åœ¨è¯¥å¤–åœºä¹‹ä¸‹è¾¾åˆ°å¹³è¡¡ï¼Œåˆ™æ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶çš„åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} f(x, E)=&\frac{1}{Q(E)} \mathrm{e}^{-\beta H(x, E)}=\frac{1}{Q(E)} \mathrm{e}^{-\beta\left[H_0(x)-A(x) E\right]} \\ Q(E)=&\int \mathrm{d} x \mathrm{e}^{-\beta\left[H_0(x)-A(x) E\right]} \end{align}$$

é€šå¸¸åšæ³•ï¼ŒæŠŠæ‰°åŠ¨ä½“ç³»çš„ç‰©ç†é‡åœ¨æœªæ‰°åŠ¨ä½“ç³»å¤„å±•å¼€ã€‚å°†æœªå—æ‰°åŠ¨çš„å¹³è¡¡æ€çš„ç³»ç»¼å‡å€¼âŸ¨â‹…âŸ©eqã€‚è‹¥å¤–åœºæ˜¯å¼±åœºï¼Œåˆ™å¯ä½œè¿‘ä¼¼å±•å¼€ï¼š $$\begin{align} \mathrm{e}^{-\beta\left[H_0(x)-A(x) E\right]}=[1+\beta AE+O(E^2)]\mathbb{e}^{-\beta H_0} \end{align}$$ äºæ˜¯ä½“ç³»é…åˆ†å‡½æ•°å±•å¼€ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} Q(E)=&\int \mathrm{d} x \mathrm{e}^{-\beta\left[H_0(x)-A(x) E\right]} \\ =& \int \mathrm{d} x [1+\beta AE+O(E^2)]\mathbb{e}^{-\beta H_0} \\ =& Q[1+\beta\langle A\rangle_{eq}E+O(E^2)] \end{align}$$

å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°æ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶åˆ†å¸ƒå‡½æ•°çš„å±•å¼€ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{equation} f(x, E)=\frac{\left[1+\beta A E+O\left(E^2\right)\right] \mathrm{e}^{-\beta H_0}}{\left[1+\beta\langle A\rangle_{\mathrm{eq}} E+O\left(E^2\right)\right] Q}=\frac{1+\beta A E+O\left(E^2\right)}{1+\beta\langle A\rangle_{\mathrm{eq}} E+O\left(E^2\right)} f(x) \end{equation}$$ æ ¹æ®|x|â€„<â€„1æ—¶$\frac{1}{1+x}$çš„çº§æ•°å±•å¼€ï¼š $$\begin{align} \frac{1+\beta A E+O\left(E^2\right)}{1+\beta \langle A\rangle_{\mathrm{eq}} E+O\left(E^2\right)}= 1+\beta[A-\langle A\rangle_{eq}]E+O(E^2) \end{align}$$ å¾—åˆ°ï¼š $$\begin{align} f(x, E)=\left \{ 1+\beta[A-\langle A\rangle_{eq}]E\right\}f(x)+O(E^2) \end{align}$$ å…¶ä¸­âŸ¨AâŸ©eqä¸ºæœªæ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶å¹³è¡¡æ€Açš„å‡å€¼ï¼Œä¸å¤±æ™®éæ€§çš„å¯ä»¤âŸ¨AâŸ©eqâ€„=â€„0ï¼Œå› ä¸ºAæ˜¯æ‰°åŠ¨é¡¹çš„å…±è½­ç‰©ç†é‡ï¼Œåœ¨å¹³è¡¡æ²¡æœ‰æ‰°åŠ¨çš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è®¤ä¸ºè¯¥ç‰©ç†é‡æ˜¯ä¸å­˜åœ¨çš„ã€‚

è®¾B(x)ä¸ºä½“ç³»çš„ä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡ï¼Œæ‰°åŠ¨æ—¶å…¶å‡å€¼ä¸ºï¼š $$\begin{align} \langle B(E) \rangle =& \int dx f(x, E)B(x) \\ =&\int dx f(x)\left [ 1+\beta A(x) E\right]B(x)+O(E^2) \\ =& \langle B\rangle_{eq} +\beta\langle AB\rangle_{eq}E+O(E^2) \\ \langle \Delta B(E) \rangle \equiv& \langle B(E) \rangle -\langle B \rangle_{eq} \\ =& \chi_{BA}E+O(E^2) \\ \chi_{BA}=& \beta\langle AB\rangle_{eq} \end{align}$$ å…¶ä¸­Ï‡BAç§°ä¸ºå¹¿ä¹‰æåŒ–ç‡ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡Aä¸ºå¤–åœºEå…±è½­çš„é‚£ä¸ªä½“ç³»çš„åŠ›å­¦é‡ï¼Œå³å¤–å› Eæ˜¯é€šè¿‡å†…å› Aå¯¹ä½“ç³»çš„ä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡Bèµ·ä½œç”¨çš„ï¼Œé‚£ä¸ªä½œç”¨å°±æ˜¯å“åº”ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªä¸‹æ ‡Bã€‚è‹¥å–åŠ›å­¦é‡Bä¸ºä½“ç³»æ€»çš„ç”µå¶æçŸ©Mï¼Œåˆ™Ï‡BAå°±æ˜¯ç”µæåŒ–ç‡ã€‚å½“é«˜æ¬¡é¡¹å¯ä»¥å¿½ç•¥çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°çº¿æ€§å“åº”ä¸ºï¼š âŸ¨Î”B(E)âŸ©â€„=â€„Ï‡BAE ä¸Šå¼è¡¨ç¤ºåœ¨æ–½åŠ å¼±å¤–åœºEæ—¶ï¼Œå¤–åœºEé€šè¿‡ä¸ä½“ç³»ç§å…±è½­åŠ›å­¦é‡Açš„ç›¸äº’ä½œç”¨ï¼Œé€ æˆä»»æ„åŠ›å­¦é‡Bäº§ç”Ÿå“åº”çš„å¢é‡ã€‚å¹¿ä¹‰æåŒ–ç‡Ï‡BAè¡¨ç¤ºå•ä½å¤–åœºEé€šè¿‡Aé€ æˆåŠ›å­¦é‡Bçš„å“åº”å¢é‡ã€‚

ç”¨Rayleigh-Ritzå˜åˆ†åŸç†å¯¼å‡ºé‡å­åŠ›å­¦çš„å®šæ€Schrodingeræ–¹ç¨‹H|Î¨âŸ©â€„=â€„E|Î¨âŸ©ï¼Œä½“ç³»èƒ½é‡çš„å‡å€¼ä¸ºâŸ¨Î¨|H|Î¨âŸ©ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶ä½“ç³»æ³¢å‡½æ•°å¿…é¡»å½’ä¸€åŒ–âŸ¨Î¨|Î¨âŸ©â€„=â€„1ï¼ŒæŠŠè¿™ä¸ªå½“æˆçº¦æŸåŒæ—¶åˆ©ç”¨æ”¹å˜æ³¢å‡½æ•°æ±‚èƒ½é‡å‡å€¼çš„æœ€å°å€¼ã€‚åˆ©ç”¨Lagrangeä¹˜å­æ³•ï¼Œå˜ä¸ºä¸€ä¸ªæ— çº¦æŸçš„å˜åˆ†é—®é¢˜ï¼š Î©â€„â‰¡â€„âŸ¨Î¨|H|Î¨âŸ©â€…âˆ’â€…Îµ(âŸ¨Î¨â€…âˆ£â€…Î¨âŸ©â€…âˆ’â€…1)

å…¶ä¸­ Îµ ä¸ºå¾…å®šå¸¸æ•°, å³æ‰€è°“ Lagrange å¾…å®šä¹˜å­. äºæ˜¯è¾¾åˆ°æå€¼æ—¶å¿…æœ‰ $$ 0=\frac{\partial \Omega}{\partial|\Psi\rangle}=\frac{\partial}{\partial|\Psi\rangle}\{\langle\Psi|H| \Psi\rangle-\varepsilon(\langle\Psi \mid \Psi\rangle-1)\}=H|\Psi\rangle+\left[\left\langle H^{\dagger} \Psi\right|\right]^{\dagger}-\varepsilon|\Psi\rangle-\varepsilon[\langle\Psi|]^{\dagger}, $$

äºæ˜¯å¾—åˆ° H|Î¨âŸ©â€„=â€„Îµ|Î¨âŸ©
